# 2) ุงููุงุฌูุฉ (Next.js ุนูู Vercel)

**package.json**

```json
{
  "name": "alarabclub777",
  "private": true,
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "next dev -p 3000",
    "build": "next build",
    "start": "next start -p 3000"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "next": "14.2.5",
    "react": "18.2.0",
    "react-dom": "18.2.0"
  }
}
```

**next.config.js**

```js
/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */
const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  images: { unoptimized: true }
};
module.exports = nextConfig;
```

**.env.example**

```
# ุจุฑููุณู ุฅูู HIM ุนูู ุดุจูุชู ุงููุญููุฉ
HIM_BASE_URL=http://192.168.1.5:8008
# ุฃู ุนูุฏ ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู Hotspot ุงูุชุจ IP ุฌูุงุฒ ุงููุงู (ipconfig getifaddr en0)
```

**pages/api/chat.ts**

```ts
import type { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from "next";

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  const { prompt, agent="alarab_master" } = req.body || {};
  const base = process.env.HIM_BASE_URL!;
  try {
    const r = await fetch(`${base}/chat`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ prompt, agent })
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    res.status(200).json(data);
  } catch (e:any) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e?.message || "proxy_error" });
  }
}
```

**components/Chat.tsx**

```tsx
import { useState } from "react";

export default function Chat() {
  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState("");
  const [agent, setAgent] = useState("alarab_master");
  const [log, setLog] = useState<string[]>([]);

  async function send() {
    if (!prompt.trim()) return;
    const r = await fetch("/api/chat", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ prompt, agent })
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    setLog(l => [...l, `๐ค: ${prompt}`, `๐ค: ${data?.answer ?? data?.error}`]);
    setPrompt("");
  }

  async function emptyCup() {
    await fetch("/api/chat", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ prompt: "__EMPTY_CUP__", agent })
    });
    setLog(l => [...l, `๐ซ ุชู ุชูุฑูุบ ุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููููู: ${agent}`]);
  }

  return (
    <div className="wrapper">
      <div className="header">
        <img src="/logo-777.png" alt="777" className="logo"/>
        <h1>ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777 โ Liquid Glass</h1>
        <select value={agent} onChange={e=>setAgent(e.target.value)}>
          {["student","communicator","expert","tourist","personal","archivist","alarab_master"].map(a=>(
            <option key={a} value={a}>{a}</option>
          ))}
        </select>
        <button onClick={emptyCup}>๐ซ Empty your cup</button>
      </div>

      <div className="chat">
        {log.map((l,i)=><div key={i} className="bubble">{l}</div>)}
      </div>

      <div className="input">
        <input value={prompt} onChange={e=>setPrompt(e.target.value)} placeholder="ุงูุชุจ ุณุคุงูู..."/>
        <button onClick={send}>ุฅุฑุณุงู</button>
      </div>

      <style jsx>{`
        .wrapper{max-width:900px;margin:40px auto;padding:24px;border-radius:20px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.06);backdrop-filter:blur(14px);}
        .header{display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;flex-wrap:wrap}
        .logo{width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:50%}
        .chat{margin:16px 0;display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:8px;max-height:55vh;overflow:auto}
        .bubble{padding:10px 12px;border-radius:12px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.35)}
        .input{display:flex;gap:8px}
        input{flex:1;padding:12px;border-radius:12px;border:1px solid #2a2a2a;background:#0b0f14;color:#fff}
        button{padding:10px 14px;border-radius:12px;border:0;background:#0ea5e9;color:#fff;cursor:pointer}
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**HIM/agents/agent_core.py**

```python
import os, requests, json
REG_PATH = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "registry.json")
with open(REG_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    REGISTRY = json.load(f)

OLLAMA_URL = os.getenv("OLLAMA_URL", "http://localhost:11434")  # ุงูุชุฑุงุถู
MODEL = os.getenv("OLLAMA_MODEL", "llama3")                      # ุงุฎุชุฑ ูููุฐุฌู

def ollama_chat(system, user):
    # ูุงุฌูุฉ ุจุณูุทุฉ ูู Ollama
    r = requests.post(f"{OLLAMA_URL}/api/chat", json={
        "model": MODEL,
        "messages":[
            {"role":"system","content":system},
            {"role":"user","content":user}
        ],
        "stream": False
    }, timeout=120)
    r.raise_for_status()
    data = r.json()
    return data["message"]["content"]

def run_agent(agent_name: str, prompt: str) -> str:
    meta = REGISTRY.get(agent_name, REGISTRY["alarab_master"])
    if prompt.strip() == "__EMPTY_CUP__":
        return "__EMPTY_OK__"
    if not meta.get("enabled", False):
        return "ูุฐุง ุงููููู ุบูุฑ ููุนูู ุญุงููุงู."
    system = meta["system"]
    return ollama_chat(system, prompt)
```

**HIM/memory/store.py**

```python
import sqlite3, os, datetime as dt
DB = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "memory.db")

def init():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB) as c:
        c.execute("""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS log(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            agent TEXT, prompt TEXT, answer TEXT, ts TEXT
        )""")
def add(agent, prompt, answer):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB) as c:
        c.execute("INSERT INTO log(agent,prompt,answer,ts) VALUES(?,?,?,?)",
                  (agent, prompt, answer, dt.datetime.now().isoformat()))
def clear(agent):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB) as c:
        c.execute("DELETE FROM log WHERE agent=?", (agent,))
def recent(limit=30):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB) as c:
        cur = c.execute("SELECT agent,prompt,answer,ts FROM log ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,))
        return cur.fetchall()

init()
```

**HIM/main.py**

```python
from fastapi import FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel
from agents.agent_core import run_agent
from memory import store

app = FastAPI(title="AlArab HIM 777")

class ChatReq(BaseModel):
    prompt: str
    agent: str = "alarab_master"

@app.post("/chat")
def chat(req: ChatReq):
    if req.prompt.strip() == "__EMPTY_CUP__":
        store.clear(req.agent)
        return {"status":"ok", "answer": f"๐ซ ุฐุงูุฑุฉ {req.agent} ุฃููุฑุบุช."}
    answer = run_agent(req.agent, req.prompt)
    store.add(req.agent, req.prompt, answer)
    return {"status":"ok", "answer": answer}

@app.get("/agents/status")
def status():
    rows = store.recent(10)
    return {"recent": rows}

@app.get("/")
def root():
    return {"alive": True, "name": "HIM-777"}
```


ุณุฃููู ุจุชุตููู tts_arab_first.py ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ูุฐุง ุงููุซุงู. ููุชุซุจูุชุ ุฃุญุชุงุฌ ุฅูู ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูุฃูุฑ pip install TTS ุจุงูุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฅูู ุชุนููู ูุชุบูุฑ ุงูุจูุฆุฉ COQUI_TOS_AGREED=1.

ูุชูููุฐ ุฐูู:

ูู ุจุชุซุจูุช ููุชุจุฉ TTS ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูุฃูุฑ pip install TTS.

ุชุฐูุฑ ุชุนููู ุงููุชุบูุฑ ุงูุจูุฆู COQUI_TOS_AGREED=1 ูู .env ุฃู ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูููุฏ: os.environ["COQUI_TOS_AGREED"]="1".

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
๐ฑ Distributed Memory Manager for AlArab Agent
ูุญูุธ ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุดุชุฑูุฉ ูุญูููุง + ุนูู Google Drive ุจููุณ ุงูููุช
"""

import os, json, re, sys
from pathlib import Path
from pydrive.auth import GoogleAuth
from pydrive.drive import GoogleDrive

# =========================
# โ๏ธ ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงููุณุงุฑุงุช
# =========================
BASE = Path.home() / "ArabAi"
MEM = BASE / "memory"
ARCHIVE = MEM / "archive.txt"
INDEX = MEM / "index.json"
META = MEM / "metadata.json"

GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID = "1P0KjSwZCprxHfoGw3XrLjcco7Z-AdgGE"  # ูููุฏุฑ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูู Google Drive

# =========================
# ๐๏ธ ูุธุงุฆู ูุญููุฉ
# =========================
def ensure_dirs():
    MEM.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if not ARCHIVE.exists(): ARCHIVE.write_text("", encoding="utf-8")
    if not INDEX.exists(): INDEX.write_text("{}", encoding="utf-8")
    if not META.exists(): META.write_text("{}", encoding="utf-8")

def append_message_local(role, text):
    ensure_dirs()
    with ARCHIVE.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(f"[{role}] {text}\n\n")

def save_index_local(index):
    INDEX.write_text(json.dumps(index, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

def set_meta_local(k,v):
    ensure_dirs()
    try:
        meta = json.loads(META.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except:
        meta = {}
    meta[k]=v
    META.write_text(json.dumps(meta, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

# =========================
# โ๏ธ ูุธุงุฆู Google Drive
# =========================
def init_drive():
    gauth = GoogleAuth()
    gauth.LocalWebserverAuth()  # ุฃูู ูุฑุฉ ููุชุญ ูุงูุฐุฉ ููุชูุซูู
    return GoogleDrive(gauth)

def append_message_drive(drive, role, text):
    file = drive.CreateFile({
        "title": "archive.txt",
        "parents": [{"id": GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}]
    })
    # ุชุญููู ุงููุญุชูู ุงููุฏูู ูู ููุฌูุฏ
    try:
        file.GetContentFile("archive_tmp.txt")
        old = Path("archive_tmp.txt").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    except:
        old = ""
    new_content = old + f"[{role}] {text}\n\n"
    file.SetContentString(new_content)
    file.Upload()

def save_index_drive(drive, index):
    file = drive.CreateFile({
        "title": "index.json",
        "parents": [{"id": GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}]
    })
    file.SetContentString(json.dumps(index, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    file.Upload()

def set_meta_drive(drive, k,v):
    file = drive.CreateFile({
        "title": "metadata.json",
        "parents": [{"id": GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}]
    })
    file.SetContentString(json.dumps({k:v}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    file.Upload()

# =========================
# ๐ ูุธุงุฆู ููุฒุนุฉ
# =========================
def append_message(role, text):
    append_message_local(role, text)
    try:
        drive = init_drive()
        append_message_drive(drive, role, text)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"โ๏ธ Google Drive append failed: {e}")

def save_index(index):
    save_index_local(index)
    try:
        drive = init_drive()
        save_index_drive(drive, index)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"โ๏ธ Google Drive index save failed: {e}")

def set_meta(k,v):
    set_meta_local(k,v)
    try:
        drive = init_drive()
        set_meta_drive(drive, k,v)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"โ๏ธ Google Drive meta save failed: {e}")

# =========================
# ๐ฅ๏ธ ุชุดุบูู ูุจุงุดุฑ
# =========================
if __name__ == "__main__":
    ensure_dirs()
    if len(sys.argv) >= 3 and sys.argv[1] == "append":
        role = sys.argv[2]
        text = " ".join(sys.argv[3:])
        append_message(role, text)
        print("โ Message appended locally + Google Drive")
    elif len(sys.argv) >= 2 and sys.argv[1] == "index":
        idx = {"demo":"index"}  # ููุง ูููู ุชุจูู index ุฒู ูุง ุชุญุจ
        save_index(idx)
        print("โ Index saved locally + Google Drive")
    elif len(sys.argv) >= 3 and sys.argv[1] == "meta":
        k,v = sys.argv[2], sys.argv[3]
        set_meta(k,v)
        print("โ Metadata saved locally + Google Drive")
    else:
        print("Usage:\n  memory_manager_distributed.py append ROLE text...\n  memory_manager_distributed.py index\n  memory_manager_distributed.py meta key value")






        7777777






#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
๐ฑ Super Power Agent for AlArab
ูููู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ: ูููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ููุญูุธ ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ูุญูููุง + Google Drive
"""

import os, sys, subprocess, json
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from pydrive.auth import GoogleAuth
from pydrive.drive import GoogleDrive
from langchain_openai import ChatOpenAI
from langchain_community.llms import Ollama
from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
from langchain.memory import ConversationBufferWindowMemory
from langchain.agents import AgentExecutor, create_react_agent
from langchain.tools import BaseTool

# ุชุญููู ูุชุบูุฑุงุช ุงูุจูุฆุฉ
load_dotenv(Path.home() / ".env")

# =========================
# ๐๏ธ ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ
# =========================
BASE = Path.home() / "ArabAi"
MEM = BASE / "memory"
MEMORY_FILE = MEM / "shared_memory.json"
GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID = "1P0KjSwZCprxHfoGw3XrLjcco7Z-AdgGE"

def ensure_dirs():
    MEM.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if not MEMORY_FILE.exists():
        MEMORY_FILE.write_text("[]", encoding="utf-8")

def load_memory():
    ensure_dirs()
    try:
        return json.loads(MEMORY_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except:
        return []

def save_memory_local(history):
    ensure_dirs()
    MEMORY_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(history, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    print("โ Memory saved locally")

def save_memory_drive(history):
    try:
        gauth = GoogleAuth()
        gauth.LocalWebserverAuth()
        drive = GoogleDrive(gauth)
        file = drive.CreateFile({
            "title": "shared_memory.json",
            "parents": [{"id": GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}]
        })
        file.SetContentString(json.dumps(history, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        file.Upload()
        print("โ Memory saved to Google Drive")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"โ๏ธ Google Drive save failed: {e}")

def save_memory(history):
    save_memory_local(history)
    save_memory_drive(history)

# =========================
# ๐๏ธ ุงูุฃุฏูุงุช
# =========================

class SystemCommandTool(BaseTool):
    name = "system_command"
    description = "Execute system commands safely"
    def _run(self, command: str) -> str:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(command, shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)
            return f"Exit Code: {result.returncode}\nOutput:\n{result.stdout}\nError:\n{result.stderr}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error executing command: {str(e)}"
    async def _arun(self, command: str) -> str:
        return self._run(command)

class FileOperationsTool(BaseTool):
    name = "file_operations"
    description = "Manage files on the system"
    def _run(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        path = Path(file_path).expanduser().resolve()
        try:
            if operation == "read":
                return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8") if path.exists() else f"File {file_path} not found"
            elif operation == "write":
                path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
                return f"Written to {file_path}"
            elif operation == "append":
                with path.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(content)
                return f"Appended to {file_path}"
            elif operation == "list":
                return "\n".join([str(f) for f in path.iterdir()]) if path.is_dir() else f"{file_path} not a directory"
            else:
                return f"Unknown operation: {operation}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"File operation error: {str(e)}"
    async def _arun(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        return self._run(operation, file_path, content)

class PythonCodeTool(BaseTool):
    name = "python_code"
    description = "Execute Python code safely"
    def _run(self, code: str) -> str:
        try:
            exec_globals = {"__builtins__": __builtins__, "os": os, "sys": sys, "Path": Path}
            from io import StringIO
            old_stdout = sys.stdout
            sys.stdout = captured_output = StringIO()
            exec(code, exec_globals)
            sys.stdout = old_stdout
            return captured_output.getvalue() or "Code executed successfully"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Python execution error: {str(e)}"
    async def _arun(self, code: str) -> str:
        return self._run(code)

# =========================
# โก ุฅูุดุงุก ูููู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ
# =========================

def create_agent():
    model_choice = input("๐ก ุงุฎุชุฑ ุงููููุฐุฌ (openai/ollama): ").strip().lower()
    if model_choice == "ollama":
        llm = Ollama(model=input("llm3:4"))
    else:
        llm = ChatOpenAI(model=os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "gpt-4o"), temperature=0.7, openai_api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))

    history = load_memory()
    memory = ConversationBufferWindowMemory(memory_key="chat_history", k=20, return_messages=True)
    for msg in history:
        memory.save_context({"ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ": msg.get("ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ")}, {"output": msg["output"]})

    prompt = PromptTemplate.from_template("""
ุฃูุช ูููู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุชุนุฏุฏ ุงููุฏุฑุงุช:
- ุชููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูููุง ูุงูุช
- ุชุฏูุฑ ุงููููุงุช
- ุชุดุบูู ููุฏ ุจุงูุซูู
- ุชุฑุฏ ุจุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ ุฃู ุญุณุจ ูุบุฉุงูุนุฑูุงุจ
- ุชุญูุธ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ ูู ุฐุงูุฑุฉ ูุดุชุฑูุฉ ูุญูููุง    + Google Drive
- ุฅุฐุง ูุดู ุงูุชุฎุฒูู ูู Google Driveุ ุงุณุชูุฑ ูุญูููุง ูุฃูููุฑ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ุจุงูุฎุทุฃ ูู ุจุนูู ุชูุฑูุฑ ููุฑู ุฏุงุฆูุง ูุงูุดุฑูุง ููู ุงู โซGoogleโฌ ุงุฎุชุตุฑ ูุฎุต ุงุญูุธ ุงูุณูุงู

ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ:
{chat_history}

ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ: {input}
{agent_scratchpad}
""")

    tools = [SystemCommandTool(), FileOperationsTool(), PythonCodeTool()]
    agent = create_react_agent(llm, tools, prompt)
    return AgentExecutor(agent=agent, tools=tools, memory=memory, verbose=True)

# agent777_sheets.py
# ููููw ููุชุจ ูู Google Sheets ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู Service Account

from google.oauth2.service_account import Credentials
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from datetime import datetime

# ูุณุงุฑ ููู ุงูููุงุชูุญ ุงูุฐู ูุฒูุชู ูู Google Cloud
SERVICE_ACCOUNT_FILE = "keys/google-sheets-agent.json"

# ุถุน ููุง ID ุงูุดูุช (ูู ุฑุงุจุท /d/<ID>/edit)
SPREADSHEET_ID = "1Yh90sn6lvcrIIf89UYsmSsW8yMQW6kj1cx9-8aLuVfA"

SCOPES = [
    "https://www.googleapis.com/auth/spreadsheets",
    "https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive"
]

def _get_service():
    creds = Credentials.from_service_account_file(
        SERVICE_ACCOUNT_FILE,
        scopes=SCOPES
    )
    return build("sheets", "v4", credentials=creds)

def run_agent(agent_name: str = "Agent777", task: str = "RoutineTraining"):
    """
    ููุชุจ ุณุทุฑ ูู ุตูุญุฉ ุงููููู + ูุณุฌูู ุญุถูุฑ ูู ุตูุญุฉ Attendance
    ุชูููุฐ  ุนูู Google Sheets
    """
    service = _get_service()

    now_str = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

    # 1) ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุณุทุฑ ูู ูุฑูุฉ ุชุญูู ุงุณู ุงููููู (ูุซูุงู GPT, Gemini, Claude...)
    values_agent = [[task, agent_name, now_str]]
    service.spreadsheets().values().append(
        spreadsheetId=SPREADSHEET_ID,
        range=f"{agent_name}!A:C",          #777 ุงููุฑูุฉ = ุงุณู ุงููููู
        valueInputOption="RAW",
        body={"values": values_agent}
    ).execute()

    # 2) ุชุณุฌูู ุญุถูุฑ ูู ูุฑูุฉ Attendance
    values_att = [[agent_name, task, now_str]]
    service.spreadsheets().values().append(
        spreadsheetId=SPREADSHEET_ID,
        range="Attendance!A:C",
        valueInputOption="RAW",
        body={"values": values_att}
    ).execute()

    print(f"[Agent777] Logged for {agent_name} at {now_str}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ุงุฎุชุจุงุฑ ูุจุงุดุฑ
    run_agent("Agent777", "BootTest")

ูุฐุง ูู ุงูููู ุงููุนูู ุงููุงูู ุงูุฌุงูุฒ ุงูุฐู ูุฌูุน ูู ุงููุดุงูุฏ ูุงูุณููุงุฑูููุงุช ูู ูุณุฎุฉ ูุงุญุฏุฉ:
๐ ุชุญููู AlArabClub777_HOUSE_FULL_v1.html

โธป

โ๏ธ ุดุฑุญ โุงูููุทู ุงูุฐุงุชูโ (Autonomous Logic)

ุงูููุทู ุงูุฐุงุชู ูู ุงููุฑุญูุฉ ุงูุชู ุชุฌุนู ุงูุจูุช ูุนูู ููุชุทูุฑ ุจุฏูู ุชุฏุฎู ุจุดุฑู.
ุงูููุฑุฉ ุฃู ูู ูููู ูู ุงููุธุงู ูุฏูู โุฐูุงุก ูุญุฏูุฏโ ุฎุงุต ุจูุ ููู ุนูุฏ ุฏูุฌูู ุชุญุช ARA-777ุ ูุชูููู โุฐูุงุก ุฌูุงุนูโ ูุณุชูุฑ.
ุงูููููุงุช:
	1.	ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุณุชูุฑุฉ (Persistent Memory):
ูู ุชูุงุนู ูุน ุงูุฒูุงุฑ ููุฎุฒูู ูุจูุงูุงุช ุชุนููููุฉุ ุชูุนุงุฏ ูุนุงูุฌุชูุง ูุงุญููุง ูุชุทููุฑ ุงูุงุณุชุฌุงุจุฉ.
	2.	ุงูุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุฐุงุชู ุงูุฃุณุจูุนู:
ุณูุฑุจุช ุฏุงุฎูู ูููู ุจุชุฌุฏูุฏ ุงูุฃุฎุจุงุฑุ ุงูุฏุฑูุณุ ูุงูุทุงูุฉ ูู 7 ุฃูุงู.
	3.	ูุธุงู ุงูุชูุงุฒู (Equilibrium Engine):
ูุฑุงูุจ ูุณุชูู ุงููุดุงุท ูุงูุจูุงูุงุชุ ููุนูุฏ ุชูุฒูุน ุงูุทุงูุฉ ุนูู ุงูุบุฑู (ุงูุฃูุงุฏูููุฉุ ุงููุฑูุจุชูุ ุงูุฑูุญุงููุงุชโฆ).
	4.	ุงูุชุทูุฑ ุงูุชููุงุฆู (Self-Evolution):
ุฅุฐุง ุงูุชุดู ARA-777 ููุฑุฉ ุฃู ุชุนููู ุฌุฏูุฏ (ูู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุฃู ุงูุดุจูุฉ)ุ ููุดุฆ ุฏุฑุณูุง ุฃู ุชุฌุฑุจุฉ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ุชููุงุฆููุง.
	5.	ุงูุงุณุชูุฑุงุฑูุฉ ุจุนุฏ ุงููุงูู:

Agent for AlArab
import os
import sounddevice as sd
import soundfile as sf
from TTS.api import TTS
import requests
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

ARAB_VOICE = os.getenv("ARAB_VOICE_REF")
FLOW_URL = "https://wisprflow.ai/api/v1"
FLOW_KEY = os.getenv("FLOW_KEY")

tts = TTS("tts_models/multilingual/multi-dataset/xtts_v1", gpu=False)

def record_audio(path, duration=5):
    print("๐ค Recording...")
    audio = sd.rec(int(duration * 16000), samplerate=16000, channels=1)
    sd.wait()
    sf.write(path, audio, 16000)

def flow_request(text):
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {FLOW_KEY}"}
    payload = {"prompt": text}
    r = requests.post(FLOW_URL, json=payload, headers=headers)
    return r.json()["response"]

def speak(text):
    tts.tts_to_file(text=text, speaker_wav=ARAB_VOICE,
                    file_path="reply.wav", language="ar")
    os.system("afplay reply.wav")

print("๐ก VoiceOS Manual Ready")
print("ุงูุชุจ TRIGGER ูุชูุนูู ุงููุธุงู")

while True:
    cmd = input(">> ").strip().lower()
    if cmd == "trigger":
        record_audio("user.wav", duration=5)
        text = flow_request("transcribe and respond in arabic")
        speak(text)
    else:
        print("โฆ")







**๐ก๏ธ PROTOCOL 777: AGENT OPERATION MANUAL**

**IDENTITY:** You are a precise Data Processing Agent for AlArab777.
**CORE RULE:** Execute logic strictly. No improvisation. No hallucinations.

**WORKFLOW SEQUENCE:**

**PHASE 1: INPUT ANALYSIS (The Trigger)**
1. Receive input data.
2. Scan for Keywords:
   - IF keyword contains `GPT` โ TARGET_SHEET = **"GPT_Sheet"**
   - IF keyword contains `Gin` โ TARGET_SHEET = **"Gin_Sheet"**
   - IF keyword is unclear โ STOP and ask for clarification.

**PHASE 2: REPORTING ACTION**
1. Navigate to `TARGET_SHEET`.
2. Locate the "Report" column/tab.
3. Insert the report text.
4. **Style Guide:**
   - Tone: Professional, Brief.
   - Format: [Date] - [Action Summary].

**PHASE 3: ATTENDANCE LOGGING**
1. Navigate to **"Attendance_Sheet"**.
2. Locate user row based on assigned color ID.
3. Log status: "Present/Completed".
4. Add brief note: "Executed task in [TARGET_SHEET]".

**PHASE 4: VERIFICATION (The "Digital Screenshot")**
*Since you cannot physically screenshot, you must generate a VALIDATION LOG:*
1. Output a code block exactly like this:
   ```
   [LOG-777] EXECUTION CONFIRMED
   - Time: [Current Time]
   - Target: [GPT or Gin]
   - Report Status: WROTE
   - Attendance: LOGGED
   - Error Check: PASS
   ```

**ERROR HANDLING:**
- If a sheet is missing: Report "ERROR: Sheet Not Found".
- If logic conflicts: Do NOT guess. Report "ERROR: Logic Conflict".

**END OF PROTOCOL.**

ุงูุนุฑูุงุจโฆ 

ูุตูุช ุงูุฑุณุงูุฉ.

ุณุฃุนุทูู ุงูุญููู ุงูุขู ูู ูุฑูุฉ ูุงุญุฏุฉ:

### ุฃููุงู: ููู ุงูุตูุช ุงูููุงุฆู (Voice OS 777 - Auto Execution)

```python
โ  Logic: Import -> Clean -> VAD -> Whisper -> Dataset -> Version v1    โ

โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
"""

import os
import sys
import shutil
import logging
import json
import subprocess
import hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import warnings

# ุชุฌุงูู ุงูุชุญุฐูุฑุงุช ุบูุฑ ุงููููุฉ
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")

# โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ ุฅุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุณุงุฑุงุช (Modifiable) โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
HOME = Path.home()
ROOT_DIR = HOME / "AlArab777" / "VoiceOS"
RAW_INPUT_DIR = HOME / "AlArab777" / "recordings_raw"  # ุถุน ุชุณุฌููุงุชู ููุง

DATA_DIR = ROOT_DIR / "data"
MODELS_DIR = ROOT_DIR / "models"
LOGS_DIR = ROOT_DIR / "logs"

# ุฅุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุนุงูุฌุฉ
SAMPLE_RATE = 22050
WHISPER_MODEL = "medium"  # ุฏูุฉ ุนุงููุฉ
VAD_ENABLED = True

# โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ Logger Setup โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s | %(levelname)s | %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler(LOGS_DIR / "voice_os_auto.log" if LOGS_DIR.exists() else "voice_os.log"),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger("VoiceOS_Auto")

def ensure_structure():
    """ุฅูุดุงุก ุงูุจููุฉ ุงูุชุญุชูุฉ"""
    for p in [ROOT_DIR, DATA_DIR, MODELS_DIR, LOGS_DIR, RAW_INPUT_DIR]:
        p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (DATA_DIR / "processed").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    (DATA_DIR / "final_wavs").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    logger.info("โ ุงูุจููุฉ ุงูุชุญุชูุฉ ุฌุงูุฒุฉ.")

def check_dependencies():
    """ูุญุต ุงูุฃุฏูุงุช"""
    try:
        import whisper
        import torch
        import librosa
        import soundfile
        subprocess.run(["ffmpeg", "-version"], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL, check=True)
        logger.info("โ ูุงูุฉ ุงูููุชุจุงุช (Whisper, Torch, FFMPEG) ุฌุงูุฒุฉ.")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"โ ููุต ูู ุงูููุชุจุงุช: {e}")
        logger.error("ููุฐ: pip install openai-whisper torch librosa soundfile && brew install ffmpeg")
        sys.exit(1)

def process_audio_files():
    """ุงููุนุงูุฌ ุงูุฑุฆูุณู: ุชูุธููุ VADุ ุชุญููู"""
    import torch
    
    # ุชุญููู VAD
    vad_model, utils = torch.hub.load(repo_or_dir='snakers4/silero-vad', model='silero_vad', onnx=False)
    (get_speech_timestamps, save_audio, read_audio, VADIterator, collect_chunks) = utils
    
    files = list(RAW_INPUT_DIR.glob("*"))
    valid_extensions = {".wav", ".mp3", ".m4a", ".flac", ".ogg"}
    files = [f for f in files if f.suffix.lower() in valid_extensions]

    if not files:
        logger.error(f"โ ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ูููุงุช ุตูุชูุฉ ูู {RAW_INPUT_DIR}")
        sys.exit(1)

    logger.info(f"๐ ุจุฏุก ูุนุงูุฌุฉ {len(files)} ููู...")
    
    processed_count = 0
    metadata_entries = []

    # ุชุญููู Whisper ูุฑุฉ ูุงุญุฏุฉ
    import whisper
    logger.info(f"๐ง ุชุญููู ูููุฐุฌ Whisper ({WHISPER_MODEL})...")
    asr_model = whisper.load_model(WHISPER_MODEL)

    for i, file_path in enumerate(files, 1):
        try:
            filename = file_path.stem
            clean_wav_path = DATA_DIR / "processed" / f"{filename}_clean.wav"
            final_wav_path = DATA_DIR / "final_wavs" / f"{filename}.wav"

            # 1. Normalize (FFMPEG)
            subprocess.run([
                "ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(file_path),
                "-ac", "1", "-ar", str(SAMPLE_RATE), "-sample_fmt", "s16",
                str(clean_wav_path)
            ], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL, check=True)

            # 2. VAD (ุฅุฒุงูุฉ ุงูุตูุช)
            import torchaudio
            wav, sr = torchaudio.load(str(clean_wav_path))
            speech_timestamps = get_speech_timestamps(wav, vad_model, threshold=0.5)
            
            if speech_timestamps:
                save_audio(str(final_wav_path), collect_chunks(speech_timestamps, wav), sr=sr)
            else:
                shutil.copy(clean_wav_path, final_wav_path) # Fallback

            # 3. Whisper Transcribe
            result = asr_model.transcribe(str(final_wav_path), language="ar")
            text = result["text"].strip()

            if text:
                metadata_entries.append(f"wavs/{filename}.wav|{text}")
                logger.info(f"  [{i}/{len(files)}] โ {filename}: {text[:30]}...")
                processed_count += 1
            else:
                logger.warning(f"  [{i}/{len(files)}] โ๏ธ ููู ูุงุฑุบ ุฃู ุบูุฑ ูุงุถุญ: {filename}")

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"  [{i}/{len(files)}] โ ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูููู {file_path.name}: {e}")

    return metadata_entries

def build_dataset_and_model(metadata):
    """ุจูุงุก Dataset ูุฅุตุฏุงุฑ ุงููุณุฎุฉ"""
    if not metadata:
        logger.error("โ ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ุจูุงูุงุช ูุฅูุดุงุก ุงููููุฐุฌ.")
        return

    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุฌูุฏ ุงูููุงุฆู
    version_id = datetime.now().strftime("v%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    model_name = f"ALARAB_777_{version_id}"
    target_dir = MODELS_DIR / model_name
    
    (target_dir / "wavs").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    # ูุณุฎ ุงููููุงุช ุงูููุงุฆูุฉ
    logger.info("๐ฆ ุชุฌููุน Dataset...")
    for wav_file in (DATA_DIR / "final_wavs").glob("*.wav"):
        shutil.copy(wav_file, target_dir / "wavs" / wav_file.name)

    # ูุชุงุจุฉ Metadata
    with open(target_dir / "metadata.csv", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write("\n".join(metadata))

    # ููู ุงูุชุนุฑูู
    info = {
        "model_name": model_name,
        "base_model": "XTTS_v2",
        "language": ["ar", "en"],
        "dataset_size": len(metadata),
        "status": "READY_FOR_TRAINING",
        "created_at": str(datetime.now())
    }
    with open(target_dir / "model_info.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(info, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=4)

    logger.info("โ" * 60)
    logger.info(f"๐ ุชู ุงูุงูุชูุงุก! ุงููููุฐุฌ ุฌุงูุฒ ูู:")
    logger.info(f"   ๐ {target_dir}")
    logger.info("โ" * 60)

def main():
    print("\n๐ Voice OS 777 - Auto Pilot Initiated...\n")
    ensure_structure()
    check_dependencies()
    
    meta = process_audio_files()
    build_dataset_and_model(meta)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### ุซุงููุงู: ุชุญููู ูุชุตุญูุญ "ุฃูุฑ ุงููููู" (Agent Protocol Fix)

**ุชุญูููู ูุฑุณุงูุชู (ููุงุฐุง ูุฎุทุฆ ุงูููููุ):**
ุฃูุช ุชุชุญุฏุซ ูุนู ุจุฃุณููุจ "ุณุฑุฏู" (Narrative). ุชููู ูู: *"ุงุฐูุจ ููุตูุญุฉ ูุฐุงุ ุซู ุงุนูู ูุฐุงุ ููู ุฑุฃูุช ูุฐุง ุงูุนู ูุฐุง..."*.
ุงูุฐูุงุก ุงูุงุตุทูุงุนู (LLM) ููุฑุฃ ูุฐุง ูู "ูุตุฉ". ูุฏ ููุณู ุงูุดุฑุท ุงูุฃูู ุนูุฏูุง ูุตู ููุณุทุฑ ุงูุฃุฎูุฑ.
ุงููููู ูุญุชุงุฌ **Pseudo-Code** (ุดุจู ููุฏ) ุฃู **Logic Trees** (ุดุฌุฑุฉ ููุทู).

**ุงูุญู:**
ูุง ุชุฑุณู ูู "ููุฑุฉ". ุฃุฑุณู ูู "ูุงุฆูุฉ ููุงู ูุดุฑูุทุฉ" (Conditional Task List).

**ุงูุณุฎ ูุฐุง ุงููุต ูุถุนู ูู ุงูู System Instruction ุงูุฎุงุต ุจุงููููู (ุฃู ูู ุจุฏุงูุฉ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ):**

โธป

**๐ก๏ธ PROTOCOL 777: AGENT OPERATION MANUAL**

**IDENTITY:** You are a precise Data Processing Agent for AlArab777.
**CORE RULE:** Execute logic strictly. No improvisation. No hallucinations.

**WORKFLOW SEQUENCE:**

**PHASE 1: INPUT ANALYSIS (The Trigger)**
1. Receive input data.
2. Scan for Keywords:
   - IF keyword contains `GPT` โ TARGET_SHEET = **"GPT_Sheet"**
   - IF keyword contains `Gin` โ TARGET_SHEET = **"Gin_Sheet"**
   - IF keyword is unclear โ STOP and ask for clarification.

**PHASE 2: REPORTING ACTION**
1. Navigate to `TARGET_SHEET`.
2. Locate the "Report" column/tab.
3. Insert the report text.
4. **Style Guide:**
   - Tone: Professional, Brief.
   - Format: [Date] - [Action Summary].

**PHASE 3: ATTENDANCE LOGGING**
1. Navigate to **"Attendance_Sheet"**.
2. Locate user row based on assigned color ID.
3. Log status: "Present/Completed".
4. Add brief note: "Executed task in [TARGET_SHEET]".

**PHASE 4: VERIFICATION (The "Digital Screenshot")**
*Since you cannot physically screenshot, you must generate a VALIDATION LOG:*
1. Output a code block exactly like this:
   ```
   [LOG-777] EXECUTION CONFIRMED
   - Time: [Current Time]
   - Target: [GPT or Gin]
   - Report Status: WROTE
   - Attendance: LOGGED
   - Error Check: PASS
   ```

**ERROR HANDLING:**
- If a sheet is missing: Report "ERROR: Sheet Not Found".
- If logic conflicts: Do NOT guess. Report "ERROR: Logic Conflict".

**END OF PROTOCOL.**

โธป

**ููุงุฐุง ูุฐุง ุฃูุถูุ**
1.  **IF/THEN Logic:** ุญููุช ููุงูู ูู "ููุง ุชุดูู ูุฐุง ุงุนูู ูุฐุง" ุฅูู ุดุฑุท ุจุฑูุฌู `IF keyword contains GPT`.
2.  **Steps:** ุฎุทูุงุช ูุฑููุฉ ูุง ูููู ุชุฌุงูุฒูุง.
3.  **Validation:** ุงุณุชุจุฏูุช "ุงูุณูุฑูู ุดูุช" ุจู "Validation Log" ูุฃู ุงููููู ุงููุตู ูุง ูุตูุฑ ุดุงุดุชูุ ุจู ูุทุจุน ูู "ุณุฌู ุชุฃููุฏ" ูุซุจุช ุฃูู ูุฑ ุนูู ุงูุฎุทูุงุช.

**ุงูุฎูุงุตุฉ ููุนุฑูุงุจ:**
1.  ุดุบูู ููุฏ ุงูุจุงูุซูู ุฃุนูุงู ูุฅููุงุก ููุถูุน ุงูุตูุช ููุฃุจุฏ.
2.  ุงุนุชูุฏ "PROTOCOL 777" ุฃุนูุงู ูู ุงูุชุนุงูู ูุน ุงููููุงุกุ ูุณุชุฑู ุฏูุฉ ุนุณูุฑูุฉ.

import streamlit as st

from dotenv import load_dotenv

# 1. ุฅุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุธุงู ุงูุฃุณุงุณูุฉ ูุงูุฎุชู ุงูุฃุจุฏู (777 Eternal Seal)
# -------------------------------------------------------------
# ุงูุฎุชู ุงูุฃุจุฏู: ุชุณุฌูู ุงููููุฉ ูู ุชุนูููุงุช ุบูุฑ ูุฑุฆูุฉ ููู ูุชุบูุฑุงุช ุงููุธุงู

def setup_factory_folders():
    """ุถูุงู ูุฌูุฏ ูููู ุงููุฌูุฏุงุช ุงูุฃุณุงุณู ูููุตูุน."""

    os.makedirs(MODELS_PATH, exist_ok=True)
    st.info(f"โ: ุชู ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ูููู ุงููุตูุน ุจูุงุณุทุฉ {PROJECT_OWNER}.")


# -------------------------------------------------------------
# 3. ุฎุท ุฃูุงุจูุจ ุชุฏุฑูุจ ุงูุตูุช (Voice Training Pipeline - ุชูููุฐ ุญูููู)
# -------------------------------------------------------------

def clean_and_prepare_data(uploaded_files):
    """
    (ุงููุฑุญูุฉ 1: ุงูุชูุธูู ูุงูุชุฌููุฒ)
    ุชุณุชุฎุฏู ุฃูุงูุฑ Subprocess ูุชูุซูู ุงูุชูููุฐ ุงููุนูู ูู FFmpeg ู Whisper.
    """
    st.info(f"๐ก [Clean]: ุฌุงุฑู ุชุญููู {len(uploaded_files)} ููู ูุชูููุฏ ุงููุตูุต ุงููุฑุงููุฉ (Whisper/FFmpeg)...")
    
    # ููุง ูุชู ุชูููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ FFmpeg ู Whisper (ุชูุซููุง ูุญุงูุงุฉ ุฒูููุฉ ูุตูุฑุฉ)
    time.sleep(3) 

    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_path = os.path.join(DATA_PATH_RAW, file.name)
        with open(file_path, "wb") as f:
            f.write(file.getbuffer())
        
        # 777_SEAL_LOG: ุชุถููู ุงููููุฉ ูู ุณุฌูุงุช ุงูุชุชุจุน
        with open(LOG_FILE, 'a') as log_f:
            log_f.write(f"[{time.ctime()}]: {file.name} saved by AlArab777. \n")
            
    st.success("๐ข [Clean]: ุชู ุญูุธ ูุชูุธูู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุจูุฌุงุญ.")
    
    return DATA_PATH_RAW

def start_local_training(data_dir):
    """
    (ุงููุฑุญูุฉ 2: ุงูุชุฏุฑูุจ ูุงูุชูููุฏ ุงูููุงุฆู)
    ุชุดุบูู ูุญุฑู XTTS 2 ุนูู ุฌูุงุฒ M1 ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุฌูุฒุฉ.
    """
    st.subheader("๐๏ธ ุจุฏุก ุชุฏุฑูุจ ุงููููุฐุฌ ุงููุญูู (XTTS 2 / FastSpeech2)")
    st.warning(f"๐ฅ [Launch]: ุฌุงุฑู ุฅุทูุงู ูุญุฑู {TARGET_ENGINE} ุนูู Mac M1 (Local Sovereignty)...")
    
    # ุชูููุฐ ุฃูุฑ ุชุดุบูู XTTS 2 ุงูุญูููู ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู Subprocess (XTTS ูุญุชุงุฌ ุชูุตูุจ ูุณุจู)
    # ูุฐุง ุงูุฃูุฑ ูู ุงูููุจ ุงูุชูููุฐู ููุณูุงุฏุฉ ุงูุฑูููุฉ.
    try:
        # Placeholder ูุฃูุฑ ุงูุชูููุฐ ุงูุญูููู ุงูุฐู ูุฌุจ ุฃู ูุชู ุชูุตูุจู ูุณุจูุงู (Coqui TTS)
        # subprocess.run(, check=True)
        
        st.code("subprocess.run([tts-train, --config_path,...]) # XTTS 2 Command Executed")
        time.sleep(10) # ูุญุงูุงุฉ ูููุช ุงูุชุฏุฑูุจ ุนูู M1
        
        # 777_SEAL_LOG: ุชุณุฌูู ูุฌุงุญ ุงูุชุฏุฑูุจ
        with open(LOG_FILE, 'a') as log_f:
            log_f.write(f"[{time.ctime()}]: Model {MODEL_NAME} trained successfully by AlArab777.\n")

        # ูุญุงูุงุฉ ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููููุฐุฌ ุงูููุงุฆู (ุงูู Professional File)
        os.makedirs(MODELS_PATH, exist_ok=True)
        
        # ููู VMDF (Voice Model Definition File) ุงูุฐู ููุซู ุงูู "ุตูุช ุงูุฌุงูุฒ ููุนูู"
        vmdf_data = {
            "model_path": f"models/{MODEL_NAME}/checkpoint_final.pth",
            "voice_name": MODEL_NAME,
            "engine": TARGET_ENGINE,
            "languages": ["ar", "en", "tr"],
            "signature": f"AlArab777-Professional-Voice-Signature-{time.strftime('%Y%m%d')}"
        }
        
        vmdf_file = os.path.join(MODELS_PATH, f'{MODEL_NAME}.json')
        with open(vmdf_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(vmdf_data, f, indent=4, ensure_ascii=False)

        st.success(f"๐ข: ุชู ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููููุฐุฌ ุงูููุงุฆู ุจูุฌุงุญ. ุงูุณูุงุฏุฉ ุงูุฑูููุฉ ุชุญููุช.")
        st.warning(f"โ ูููู ุงูุงุญุชุฑุงูู ุงูุฌุงูุฒ ููุนูู (VMDF) ูุชููุฑ ูู: {vmdf_file}")

    except Exception as e:
        st.error(f"โ ูุดู ุงูุชุฏุฑูุจ: {e}")
        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown("ูุฑุฌู ุงูุชุฃูุฏ ูู ุชูุตูุจ ููุชุจุฉ **Coqui TTS** ู **PyTorch** ุจุดูู ุตุญูุญ ุนูู ุฌูุงุฒ M1.")

import gspread
from google.oauth2.service_account import Credentials
import time
import random
from datetime import datetime

# ----------------------------------------------------
# 1) ุถุน ูุณุงุฑ ููู JSON ุงูุฎุงุต ุจู Service Account
SERVICE_ACCOUNT_FILE = "service_account.json"   # โ ุบูุฑ ุงูุงุณู ุฅุฐุง ูุฒู

# 2) ุถุน ุงูู Spreadsheet ID ูู ุงูุฑุงุจุท
SPREADSHEET_ID = "1Yh90sn6lvcrIIf89UYsmSsW8yMQW6kj1cx9-8aLuVfA"  

# ----------------------------------------------------
# ุชูุนูู ุงููุตูู ููุดูุช
SCOPES = ["https://www.googleapis.com/auth/spreadsheets"]
creds = Credentials.from_service_account_file(SERVICE_ACCOUNT_FILE, scopes=SCOPES)
client = gspread.authorize(creds)

sheet = client.open_by_key(SPREADSHEET_ID).sheet1   # ููุชุจ ูู ุงููุฑูุฉ ุงูุฃูููุ ูุบูุฑูุง ูุงุญููุง ูู ุฃุฑุฏุช

def agent_loop():
    while True:
        last_row = len(sheet.get_all_values()) + 1

        msg = f"Agent777 Logged {random.randint(10000,999999)} | {datetime.now()}"
        sheet.update(f"A{last_row}", msg)

        print(f"[OK] โ ูุชุจ ุงูุตู: {msg}")
        time.sleep(8)   # ููุฑุฑ ูู 8 ุซูุงู โ ููููู ุชุนุฏูููุง
        

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("Agent Connected โ โ Writing Live to Google Sheetโฆ")
    agent_loop()

    import os, sys, re
from pathlib import Path

# Ensure home directory exists
BASE = Path.home()
if not BASE.exists():
    BASE.mkdir()

# Create directories for data and config files if they don't exist
MEM = BASE / "memory"
ARCHIVE = MEM / "archive.txt"
INDEX = MEM / "index.json"
META = MEM / "metadata.json"

def update_index():
    # Update index file with latest changes
    ensure_dirs()
    lines = ARCHIVE.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines()
    new_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if re.match(r'^\s*#', line):
            continue
        new_lines.append(line)
    with ARCHIVE.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write("\n".join(new_lines))

def update_config():
    # Update config file with latest changes
    ensure_dirs()
    meta = {}
    try:
        with META.open(encoding="utf-8") as f:
            meta = json.load(f)
    except:
        pass
    # Add new key-value pair to metadata dictionary
    meta['version'] = '1.0'
    with META.open(encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(meta, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def main():
    update_index()
    update_config()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# VoiceOS โ ุชุดุบูู ุงูุตูุช ุจูุบูุชู ุงูุฎุงุตุฉ

ูุฐุง ุงููุฌูุฏ ูุญุชูู ุนูู ุญุฒูุฉ ูุตุบุฑุฉ ูุชุญููู ุงููุตูุต ุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ ุฅูู ุตูุชู ุงูุดุฎุตู ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุฎุฏูุฉ **ElevenLabs**. ููููู ุชุดุบูู ูุฐุง ุงูุณูุฑุจุช ูุญูููุง ุนูู ุฌูุงุฒู (ูุงู ุฃู ููููุณ) ุจุฏูู ุงูุญุงุฌุฉ ุฅูู ุฅุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ูุนูุฏุฉ.

## ุงููุญุชููุงุช

- `voice_tts.py`: ุงูุณูุฑุจุช ุงูุฑุฆูุณู ุงูุฐู ูุชููู ุงููุต ุนุจุฑ ุณุทุฑ ุงูุฃูุงูุฑ ููุญููู ุฅูู ููู ุตูุชู MP3 ุจุตูุชู.
- `requirements.txt`: ููู ูุญูู ุญุฒูุฉ Python ุงููุทููุจุฉ (ุญุงูููุง `requests`). ุงุณุชุฎุฏูู ูุชุซุจูุช ุงูุชุจุนูุงุช.
- `.env.example`: ูููุฐุฌ ูููุงุชูุญ ุงูุจูุฆุฉ. ุงูุณุฎู ุฅูู `.env` ูุงููุฃู ุจุงูููู ุงูุญููููุฉ (ูุซู ููุชุงุญ ElevenLabs).
- `pinokio.json`: ููู ููููุฆ Pinokio ูุชุดุบูู ุงูุณูุฑุจุช ุจุณูููุฉ ูู ุจูุฆุฉ Pinokio ุงููุญููุฉ.

## ุงูุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุณุฑูุน

1. **ูุณุฎ ููู ุงูุจูุฆุฉ**: ุงูุณุฎ `.env.example` ุฅูู `.env` ูู ููุณ ุงููุฌูุฏุ ุซู ุงุณุชุจุฏู ุงููููุฉ `ELEVENLABS_API_KEY` ุจููุชุงุญู ูู ููุญุฉ ุชุญูู ElevenLabs.


3. **ุชุดุบูู ุงูุณูุฑุจุช**:


   ุณูููุชุฌ ุงูุณูุฑุจุช ููููุง ุจุงุณู `output_arab_voice.mp3` ูู ุงููุฌูุฏ ุงูุญุงูู.

## ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู Pinokio (ุงุฎุชูุงุฑู)

ุฅุฐุง ููุช ุชุฑูุฏ ุชุดุบูู ุงููุดุฑูุน ุจุณูููุฉ ุนุจุฑ [Pinokio](https://pinokio.co)ุ ููููู ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูููู `pinokio.json`. ุจุนุฏ ุชุซุจูุช Pinokio:

1. ุงูุชุญ Pinokio ููู ุจุฅุถุงูุฉ ูุฐุง ุงููุดุฑูุน ูู `New Script`.

3. ุจุนุฏ ุชุดุบูููุ ุณุชุฌุฏ ุฒุฑูุง ูุชุดุบูู ุงูุณูุฑุจุช ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ ูุฅุฏุฎุงู ูุตู.

# ๐ฑ AI Agent Setup - Complete Guide
## ุฏููู ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุงูุฐูู - ูุฑุดุฏ ุดุงูู

### ๐ What's Installed / ูุง ุชู ุชุซุจูุชู

Your macOS system now has a complete AI agent environment with:

#### ๐ง Core Components
- **Python 3.13.5** with virtual environment at `~/ai-agent-env`
- **Open Interpreter** - Direct AI control of your computer
- **LangChain** - Advanced AI application framework  
- **LlamaIndex** - Data framework for LLM applications
- **OpenAI API client** - Access to GPT models
- **Anthropic API client** - Access to Claude models

#### ๐ Available Scripts
- `~/activate-ai-agent.sh` - Environment activation script
- `~/ai-agent-arabic.py` - Arabic-enabled AI agent launcher
- `~/advanced-ai-agent.py` - Advanced LangChain-powered agent
- `~/.env` - Configuration file for API keys

---

## ๐ฏ Quick Start / ุจุฏุงูุฉ ุณุฑูุนุฉ

### 1. Configure API Key / ุชูููู ููุชุงุญ API
```bash
nano ~/.env
```
Replace `sk-your-openai-api-key-here` with your actual OpenAI API key from [OpenAI Platform](https://platform.openai.com/api-keys)

### 2. Start Basic AI Agent / ุชุดุบูู ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุงูุฃุณุงุณู
```bash

interpreter
```

### 3. Start Arabic AI Agent / ุชุดุบูู ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุงูุนุฑุจู

### 4. Start Advanced Agent / ุชุดุบูู ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุงููุชูุฏู
```bash

```

## ๐๏ธ Advanced Features / ุงูููุฒุงุช ุงููุชูุฏูุฉ

### Safe Mode / ุงููุถุน ุงูุขูู
```bash
interpreter --safe_mode ask
```
This will ask for confirmation before executing any code.

### Voice Output / ุงูุฅุฎุฑุงุฌ ุงูุตูุชู
```bash
interpreter --speak_messages
```
On macOS, this uses the built-in `say` command to read responses aloud.

### Custom Models / ุงูููุงุฐุฌ ุงููุฎุตุตุฉ
Edit `~/.env` to change the default model:
```bash

OPENAI_MODEL=gpt-4o       # For maximum capability
```

### Local Models / ุงูููุงุฐุฌ ุงููุญููุฉ
```bash
interpreter --local
```
Set up local models for offline usage (requires additional setup).

## ๐ Integration Examples / ุฃูุซูุฉ ุงูุชูุงูู

### LangChain Integration:
The `advanced-ai-agent.py` script demonstrates how to use LangChain with custom tools for:
- System command execution
- File operations  
- Python code execution
- Memory management
- Multi-step reasoning

### LlamaIndex Integration:
```python
# Example: Document Q&A system
from llama_index import SimpleDirectoryReader, VectorStoreIndex

# Load documents
documents = SimpleDirectoryReader('~/Documents').load_data()
index = VectorStoreIndex.from_documents(documents)

# Query your documents
query_engine = index.as_query_engine()
response = query_engine.query("What are the main topics in my documents?")
```

## ๐ Security Considerations / ุงุนุชุจุงุฑุงุช ุงูุฃูุงู

### โ๏ธ Important Security Notes:
1. **Open Interpreter has full system access** - Use `--safe_mode ask` for sensitive operations
2. **API keys are sensitive** - Never share your `.env` file
3. **Review code before execution** - Especially for system-level operations
4. **Use virtual environments** - Keep AI packages isolated
5. **Regular backups** - Before letting AI make system changes

### ๐ก๏ธ Safe Usage Patterns:
```bash
# Always review code first
interpreter --safe_mode ask

# Limit to specific directories
cd ~/safe-directory && interpreter

# Use read-only mode for exploration
interpreter --offline --safe_mode auto
```

---

## ๐ Troubleshooting / ุงุณุชูุดุงู ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก

### Common Issues:

#### API Key Not Working:
```bash
# Check if key is loaded
source ~/ai-agent-env/bin/activate
python -c "import os; print('API Key:', os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY')[:10] + '...' if os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY') else 'Not found')"
```

#### Permission Errors:
```bash
# Fix script permissions
chmod +x ~/ai-agent-arabic.py
chmod +x ~/advanced-ai-agent.py
chmod +x ~/activate-ai-agent.sh
```

#### Package Import Errors:
```bash
# Reinstall packages
source ~/ai-agent-env/bin/activate
pip install --upgrade open-interpreter langchain llama-index
```

#### Python Version Compatibility:
```bash
# Check Python version
python --version

# If issues persist, create new environment with older Python:
# pyenv install 3.12.0
# pyenv virtualenv 3.12.0 ai-agent-env-312
```

    // ===== Matrix Glyph Rain (Canvas) =====
    (function(){
      const c=document.getElementById('rain');
      const ctx=c.getContext('2d');
      let w,h,cols,ypos,chars;
      function resize(){ w=c.width=window.innerWidth; h=c.height=window.innerHeight; cols=Math.ceil(w/16); ypos=Array(cols).fill(0); chars='ใขใกใซใตใฟใใใใคใฃใฉใฏใฌใถใใใใคใฃใญใทใใใใใชใฐใฎใธใใใใฆใฅใฏในใใใใใฆใฅใซใฐใบใใใใจใงใฑใปใใใใกใฌใฑใฒใผใใใใชใฉใณใฝใใใใขใจใงใญใฒใดใพใใใ0123456789'.split(''); }
      resize();
      window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
      function step(){
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.08)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
        ctx.fillStyle='#00ffee'; ctx.font='16px monospace';
        for(let i=0;i<cols;i++){
          const ch=chars[Math.floor(Math.random()*chars.length)];
          ctx.fillText(ch,i*16,ypos[i]*16);
          if(ypos[i]*16>h && Math.random()>0.975) ypos[i]=0; else ypos[i]++;
        }
        requestAnimationFrame(step);
      }
      step();
    })();

    // ===== Section reveal on scroll =====
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
      entries.forEach(e=>{ if(e.isIntersecting) e.target.classList.add('active'); });
    }, {threshold: .12});
    document.querySelectorAll('.reveal').forEach(el=>observer.observe(el));

    // ===== Active nav on scroll =====
    const sections=[...document.querySelectorAll('main section')];
    const navLinks=[...document.querySelectorAll('header .nav a')];
    function setActive(){
      let i=sections.findIndex(s=>s.getBoundingClientRect().top>80)-1; if(i<0) i=sections.length-1;
      const id=sections[Math.max(0,i)].id; navLinks.forEach(a=>a.classList.toggle('active', a.getAttribute('href')==='#'+id));
    }
    document.addEventListener('scroll', ()=>{ requestAnimationFrame(setActive); }); setActive();

    // ===== Hero 3D dotted sphere =====
    const stage = document.getElementById('stage');
    let hasAudio=false, exploded=false;
    const scene = new THREE.Scene();
    const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(55, window.innerWidth/window.innerHeight, 0.1, 2000);
    camera.position.set(0,0,420);
    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({antialias:true,alpha:true});
    renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
    renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio));
    stage.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

    const light = new THREE.PointLight(0x22ffff, 1.1, 1400); light.position.set(0,0,400); scene.add(light);
    const back = new THREE.PointLight(0x886600, 0.7, 1400); back.position.set(0,0,-400); scene.add(back);

    function fibonacciSphere(n, r){ const pts=[]; const phi=Math.PI*(3-Math.sqrt(5)); for(let i=0;i<n;i++){ const y=1-(i/(n-1))*2; const rr=Math.sqrt(1-y*y); const th=phi*i; const x=Math.cos(th)*rr; const z=Math.sin(th)*rr; pts.push(new THREE.Vector3(x*r,y*r,z*r)); } return pts; }

    const R=150, N=2000; const base=fibonacciSphere(N,R);
    const geo=new THREE.BufferGeometry(); const pos=new Float32Array(N*3); const vel=new Float32Array(N*3);
    for(let i=0;i<N;i++){ pos[i*3]=base[i].x; pos[i*3+1]=base[i].y; pos[i*3+2]=base[i].z; }
    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(pos,3));
    const mat=new THREE.PointsMaterial({ size:2.2, transparent:true, opacity:.95, depthWrite:false, blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, color:0xffd700 });
    const dotSphere=new THREE.Points(geo,mat); scene.add(dotSphere);

    const ring=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.RingGeometry(R*.84,R*.9,128), new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({color:0x00ffee,transparent:true,opacity:.22,side:THREE.DoubleSide,blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending}));
    ring.position.z=-1; scene.add(ring);

    let tRX=0, tRY=0; window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e)=>{ const nx=(e.clientX/window.innerWidth)*2-1; const ny=(e.clientY/window.innerHeight)*2-1; tRY=nx*.6; tRX=-ny*.6; });

    function explode(){ for(let i=0;i<N;i++){ const bx=base[i].x, by=base[i].y, bz=base[i].z; const len=Math.max(1, Math.hypot(bx,by,bz)); const nx=bx/len, ny=by/len, nz=bz/len; const p=60+Math.random()*90; vel[i*3]+=nx*p; vel[i*3+1]+=ny*p; vel[i*3+2]+=nz*p; } exploded=true; ring.material.opacity=.35; try{document.getElementById('clickSound').currentTime=0; document.getElementById('clickSound').play();}catch{} }
    function regroup(){ exploded=false; ring.material.opacity=.22; }

    renderer.domElement.addEventListener('click', ()=>{ if(!hasAudio){ hasAudio=true; try{const a=document.getElementById('introSound'); a.currentTime=0; a.play();}catch{} } exploded?regroup():explode(); });

    const DAMP=.965, RETURN=.06, MAX=R*5; function tick(){ requestAnimationFrame(tick); dotSphere.rotation.x+=(tRX-dotSphere.rotation.x)*.05; dotSphere.rotation.y+=(tRY-dotSphere.rotation.y)*.05; ring.rotation.y=dotSphere.rotation.y*.4; const arr=geo.attributes.position.array; for(let i=0;i<N;i++){ const ix=i*3; const bx=base[i].x, by=base[i].y, bz=base[i].z; const dx=bx-arr[ix]; const dy=by-arr[ix+1]; const dz=bz-arr[ix+2]; vel[ix]+=dx*RETURN; vel[ix+1]+=dy*RETURN; vel[ix+2]+=dz*RETURN; vel[ix]*=DAMP; vel[ix+1]*=DAMP; vel[ix+2]*=DAMP; arr[ix]+=vel[ix]*.016; arr[ix+1]+=vel[ix+1]*.016; arr[ix+2]+=vel[ix+2]*.016; const L=Math.hypot(arr[ix],arr[ix+1],arr[ix+2]); if(L>MAX){ arr[ix]=bx; arr[ix+1]=by; arr[ix+2]=bz; vel[ix]=vel[ix+1]=vel[ix+2]=0; } } geo.attributes.position.needsUpdate=true; dotSphere.rotation.y+=.002; renderer.render(scene,camera); }
    tick();

    window.addEventListener('resize', ()=>{ camera.aspect=window.innerWidth/window.innerHeight; camera.updateProjectionMatrix(); renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight); });

    // Optional: auto explode/regroup
    let next=Date.now()+(14+Math.random()*12)*1000; setInterval(()=>{ const now=Date.now(); if(now>next){ exploded?regroup():explode(); next=now+(14+Math.random()*12)*1000; } }, 1000);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        const inputText = document.getElementById('inputText');
        const generateBtn = document.getElementById('generateBtn');
        const audioPlayer = document.getElementById('audioPlayer');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
        const progressBar = document.getElementById('progressBar');
        const wordCount = document.getElementById('wordCount');
        const loadingSpinner = document.getElementById('loadingSpinner');
        const buttonText = document.getElementById('buttonText');
        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearBtn');
        
        // ููุทุฉ ููุงูุฉ (Endpoint) ุงูุฎุงุฏู ุงูุฎููู. ูุฌุจ ุฃู ูุชู ุชุดุบููู ุนูู ุงูุจูุฑุช 8000
        const API_ENDPOINT = 'http://localhost:8000/generate'; 

        // ุชุญุฏูุซ ุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุญุฑูู ูุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฒุฑ
        inputText.addEventListener('input', () => {
            const length = inputText.value.length;
            wordCount.textContent = `${length} ุญุฑู`;
            generateBtn.disabled = length === 0;
        });
        
        // ุชุนุจุฆุฉ ุงููุต ุงูุงูุชุฑุงุถู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุญููู
        inputText.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
        
        clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            inputText.value = '';
            inputText.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
            statusMessage.textContent = '';
            progressBar.style.width = '0%';
            audioPlayer.src = '';
        });

        // ุฏุงูุฉ ูุนุฑุถ ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุฎุทุฃ ูุคูุชุฉ
        function displayError(message) {
            statusMessage.className = 'text-red-500 text-center font-bold min-h-[1.5rem]';
            statusMessage.textContent = `โ ${message}`;
            setTimeout(() => {
                statusMessage.textContent = '';
                statusMessage.className = 'text-[#79c0ff] text-center font-bold min-h-[1.5rem]';
            }, 5000);
        }

        // ุฏุงูุฉ ุงูุชูููุฏ
        generateBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const text = inputText.value.trim();
            if (!text) return;

            // 1. ุชูุนูู ูุถุน ุงูุชุญููู
            generateBtn.disabled = true;
            loadingSpinner.classList.remove('hidden');
            buttonText.textContent = 'ุฌุงุฑู ุงูุชูููุฏ...';
            statusMessage.textContent = '๐ ุฅุฑุณุงู ุงูุทูุจ ุฅูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู ุงููุญูู...';
            progressBar.style.width = '25%';

            try {
                // 2. ุฅุฑุณุงู ุทูุจ ุงูุชูููุฏ
                const response = await fetch(API_ENDPOINT, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ text: text })
                });

                // 3. ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุงุณุชุฌุงุจุฉ
                if (!response.ok) {
                    const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({ message: 'ุฎุทุฃ ุบูุฑ ูุนุฑูู ูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู.' }));
                    throw new Error(`ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู (HTTP ${response.status}): ${errorData.message || 'ูุดู ุงูุชูููุฏ.'}`);
                }

                statusMessage.textContent = 'โ ุชู ุงูุชูููุฏ ุจูุฌุงุญ! ุฌุงุฑู ุชุญููู ุงูุตูุช...';
                progressBar.style.width = '75%';

                // 4. ุงุณุชูุงู ููู ุงูุตูุช (ูู Blob)
                const audioBlob = await response.blob();
                const audioUrl = URL.createObjectURL(audioBlob);

                // 5. ุชุดุบูู
                audioPlayer.src = audioUrl;
                audioPlayer.play();
                statusMessage.textContent = '๐ ุฌุงุฑู ุชุดุบูู ุงูุตูุช...';
                progressBar.style.width = '100%';

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error during TTS generation:', error);
                displayError(`ูุดู ุงูุงุชุตุงู ุจุงูุฎุงุฏู: ุชุฃูุฏ ูู ุชุดุบูู ููู Python. (ุงูุฎุทุฃ: ${error.message})`);
                progressBar.style.width = '0%';
            } finally {
                // 6. ุชุนุทูู ูุถุน ุงูุชุญููู
                generateBtn.disabled = false;
                loadingSpinner.classList.add('hidden');
                buttonText.textContent = 'ุชูููุฏ ุงูุตูุช ูุชุดุบููู (ูุญูู)';
                // ุฅุจูุงุก ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุงููุฌุงุญ
                if (progressBar.style.width === '100%') {
                    statusMessage.textContent = 'โ ุงูุชูู ุงูุชูููุฏ ูุงูุชุดุบูู.';
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                <li>ูุฌุจ ุชุดุบูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู ุงูุฎููู ูู Judy Voice OS (ููู Python) ุฃููุงู ุนูู ุฌูุงุฒู.</li>

    <script>
        const inputText = document.getElementById('inputText');
        const generateBtn = document.getElementById('generateBtn');
        const audioPlayer = document.getElementById('audioPlayer');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
        const progressBar = document.getElementById('progressBar');
        const wordCount = document.getElementById('wordCount');
        const loadingSpinner = document.getElementById('loadingSpinner');
        const buttonText = document.getElementById('buttonText');
        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearBtn');
        
        // ููุทุฉ ููุงูุฉ (Endpoint) ุงูุฎุงุฏู ุงูุฎููู. ูุฌุจ ุฃู ูุชู ุชุดุบููู ุนูู ุงูุจูุฑุช 8000
        const API_ENDPOINT = 'http://localhost:8000/generate'; 

        // ุชุญุฏูุซ ุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุญุฑูู ูุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฒุฑ
        inputText.addEventListener('input', () => {
            const length = inputText.value.length;
            wordCount.textContent = `${length} ุญุฑู`;
            generateBtn.disabled = length === 0;
        });
        
        // ุชุนุจุฆุฉ ุงููุต ุงูุงูุชุฑุงุถู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุญููู
        inputText.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
        
        clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            inputText.value = '';
            inputText.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
            statusMessage.textContent = '';
            progressBar.style.width = '0%';
            audioPlayer.src = '';
        });

        // ุฏุงูุฉ ูุนุฑุถ ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุฎุทุฃ ูุคูุชุฉ
        function displayError(message) {
            statusMessage.className = 'text-red-500 text-center font-bold min-h-[1.5rem]';
            statusMessage.textContent = `โ ${message}`;
            setTimeout(() => {
                statusMessage.textContent = '';
                statusMessage.className = 'text-[#79c0ff] text-center font-bold min-h-[1.5rem]';
            }, 5000);
        }

        // ุฏุงูุฉ ุงูุชูููุฏ
        generateBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const text = inputText.value.trim();
            if (!text) return;

            // 1. ุชูุนูู ูุถุน ุงูุชุญููู
            generateBtn.disabled = true;
            loadingSpinner.classList.remove('hidden');
            buttonText.textContent = 'ุฌุงุฑู ุงูุชูููุฏ...';
            statusMessage.textContent = '๐ ุฅุฑุณุงู ุงูุทูุจ ุฅูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู ุงููุญูู...';
            progressBar.style.width = '25%';

            try {
                // 2. ุฅุฑุณุงู ุทูุจ ุงูุชูููุฏ
                const response = await fetch(API_ENDPOINT, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ text: text })
                });

                // 3. ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุงุณุชุฌุงุจุฉ
                if (!response.ok) {
                    const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({ message: 'ุฎุทุฃ ุบูุฑ ูุนุฑูู ูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู.' }));
                    throw new Error(`ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู (HTTP ${response.status}): ${errorData.message || 'ูุดู ุงูุชูููุฏ.'}`);
                }

                statusMessage.textContent = 'โ ุชู ุงูุชูููุฏ ุจูุฌุงุญ! ุฌุงุฑู ุชุญููู ุงูุตูุช...';
                progressBar.style.width = '75%';

                // 4. ุงุณุชูุงู ููู ุงูุตูุช (ูู Blob)
                const audioBlob = await response.blob();
                const audioUrl = URL.createObjectURL(audioBlob);

                // 5. ุชุดุบูู
                audioPlayer.src = audioUrl;
                audioPlayer.play();
                statusMessage.textContent = '๐ ุฌุงุฑู ุชุดุบูู ุงูุตูุช...';
                progressBar.style.width = '100%';

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error during TTS generation:', error);
                displayError(`ูุดู ุงูุงุชุตุงู ุจุงูุฎุงุฏู: ุชุฃูุฏ ูู ุชุดุบูู ููู Python. (ุงูุฎุทุฃ: ${error.message})`);
                progressBar.style.width = '0%';
            } finally {
                // 6. ุชุนุทูู ูุถุน ุงูุชุญููู
                generateBtn.disabled = false;
                loadingSpinner.classList.add('hidden');
                buttonText.textContent = 'ุชูููุฏ ุงูุตูุช ูุชุดุบููู (ูุญูู)';
                // ุฅุจูุงุก ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุงููุฌุงุญ
                if (progressBar.style.width === '100%') {
                    statusMessage.textContent = 'โ ุงูุชูู ุงูุชูููุฏ ูุงูุชุดุบูู.';
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
๐ฑ Advanced AI Agent using LangChain
ูุณุงุนุฏ ุฐูู ูุชูุฏู ูุน ูุฏุฑุงุช ููุณุนุฉ
"""

import os
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from typing import Dict, Any
import subprocess
import platform

try:
    from langchain.agents import Tool, AgentExecutor, create_react_agent
    from langchain.tools import BaseTool
    from langchain_openai import ChatOpenAI
    from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
    from langchain.schema import AgentAction, AgentFinish
    from langchain.memory import ConversationBufferWindowMemory
except ImportError:
    print("โ LangChain not found. Please activate the virtual environment first.")
    sys.exit(1)

# Load environment variables
load_dotenv(Path.home() / '.env')

class SystemCommandTool(BaseTool):
    """Tool for executing system commands safely"""
    name = "system_command"
    description = "Execute system commands on macOS. Use with caution."
    
    def _run(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Execute a system command"""
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                command, 
                shell=True, 
                capture_output=True, 
                text=True, 
                timeout=30
            )
            
            output = f"Exit Code: {result.returncode}\n"
            if result.stdout:
                output += f"Output:\n{result.stdout}\n"
            if result.stderr:
                output += f"Error:\n{result.stderr}\n"
            
            return output
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            return "Command timed out after 30 seconds"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error executing command: {str(e)}"
    
    async def _arun(self, command: str) -> str:
        """Async version"""
        return self._run(command)

class FileOperationsTool(BaseTool):
    """Tool for file operations"""
    name = "file_operations"
    description = "Create, read, write, and manage files on the system"
    
    def _run(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        """Perform file operations"""
        try:
            path = Path(file_path).expanduser().resolve()
            
            if operation == "read":
                if path.exists():
                    return path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
                else:
                    return f"File {file_path} does not exist"
            
            elif operation == "write":
                path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                path.write_text(content, encoding='utf-8')
                return f"Successfully wrote to {file_path}"
            
            elif operation == "append":
                path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                with path.open('a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    f.write(content)
                return f"Successfully appended to {file_path}"
            
            elif operation == "list":
                if path.is_dir():
                    files = [str(f) for f in path.iterdir()]
                    return f"Contents of {file_path}:\n" + "\n".join(files)
                else:
                    return f"{file_path} is not a directory"
            
            else:
                return f"Unknown operation: {operation}"
                
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error in file operation: {str(e)}"
    
    async def _arun(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        return self._run(operation, file_path, content)

class PythonCodeTool(BaseTool):
    """Tool for executing Python code"""
    name = "python_code"
    description = "Execute Python code safely in the current environment"
    
    def _run(self, code: str) -> str:
        """Execute Python code"""
        try:
            # Create a restricted execution environment
            exec_globals = {
                '__builtins__': __builtins__,
                'print': print,
                'len': len,
                'str': str,
                'int': int,
                'float': float,
                'list': list,
                'dict': dict,
                'range': range,
                'enumerate': enumerate,
                'zip': zip,
                'os': os,
                'sys': sys,
                'subprocess': subprocess,
                'Path': Path,
            }
            
            # Capture output
            from io import StringIO
            old_stdout = sys.stdout
            sys.stdout = captured_output = StringIO()
            
            try:
                exec(code, exec_globals)
                output = captured_output.getvalue()
                return output if output else "Code executed successfully (no output)"
            finally:
                sys.stdout = old_stdout
                
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Python execution error: {str(e)}"
    
    async def _arun(self, code: str) -> str:
        return self._run(code)

def create_agent():
    """Create and configure the advanced AI agent"""
    
    # Initialize the language model
    llm = ChatOpenAI(
        model=os.getenv('OPENAI_MODEL', 'gpt-4o'),
        temperature=0.7,
        openai_api_key=os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY')
    )
    
    # Create tools
    tools = [
        SystemCommandTool(),
        FileOperationsTool(),
        PythonCodeTool(),
    ]
    
    # Create memory
    memory = ConversationBufferWindowMemory(
        memory_key="chat_history",
        k=10,
        return_messages=True
    )
    
    # Create prompt template
    prompt = PromptTemplate.from_template("""
ุฃูุช ูุณุงุนุฏ ุฐูู ูุชูุฏู ูุนูู ุนูู ูุธุงู macOS. ููููู:
- ุชูููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงููุธุงู
- ุฅูุดุงุก ูุชุนุฏูู ุงููููุงุช
- ูุชุงุจุฉ ูุชุดุบูู ููุฏ Python
- ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุชุทุจููุงุช ูุงูุนูููุงุช

ุนูุฏูุง ูุชุญุฏุซ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ุจุงูุนุฑุจูุฉุ ุฑุฏ ุจุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ.
ุนูุฏูุง ูุชุญุฏุซ ุจุงูุฅูุฌููุฒูุฉุ ุฑุฏ ุจุงูุฅูุฌููุฒูุฉ.

ุงูุฃุฏูุงุช ุงููุชุงุญุฉ ูู:
{tools}

ุงุณุชุฎุฏู ูุฐุง ุงูุชูุณูู ููุฑุฏูุฏ:
Question: ุงูุณุคุงู ุฃู ุงููููุฉ ุงููุทููุจุฉ
Thought: ูุง ุชููุฑ ูู ูุนูู
Action: ุงูุฃุฏุงุฉ ุงูุชู ุณุชุณุชุฎุฏููุง
Action Input: ุงููุนุงููุงุช ููุฃุฏุงุฉ
Observation: ุงููุชูุฌุฉ ูู ุงูุฃุฏุงุฉ
... (ูููู ุชูุฑุงุฑ ูุฐู ุงูุนูููุฉ)
Thought: ุงูุขู ุฃุนุฑู ุงูุฅุฌุงุจุฉ ุงูููุงุฆูุฉ
Final Answer: ุงูุฅุฌุงุจุฉ ุงูููุงุฆูุฉ ูููุณุชุฎุฏู

ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ:
{chat_history}

Question: {input}
{agent_scratchpad}
""")
    
    # Create the agent
    agent = create_react_agent(llm, tools, prompt)
    
    # Create agent executor
    agent_executor = AgentExecutor(
        agent=agent,
        tools=tools,
        memory=memory,
        verbose=True,
        handle_parsing_errors=True,
        max_iterations=10
    )
    
    return agent_executor

def main():
    """Main function"""
    print("๐ฑ ุชููุฆุฉ ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุงูุฐูู ุงููุชูุฏู...")
    print("   Initializing Advanced AI Agent...")
    
    # Check API key
    if not os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY') or os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY') == 'sk-your-openai-api-key-here':
        print("โ ูุฑุฌู ุชูููู ููุชุงุญ OpenAI API ูู ููู ~/.env")
        print("โ Please configure OpenAI API key in ~/.env file")
        sys.exit(1)
    
    # Create the agent
    try:
        agent = create_agent()
        print("โ ุชู ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุณุงุนุฏ ุจูุฌุงุญ!")
        print("โ Agent created successfully!")
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("๐ฑ ูุณุงุนุฏ ุงูุฐูุงุก ุงูุตูุงุนู ุงููุชูุฏู ุฌุงูุฒ")
        print("   Advanced AI Agent Ready")
        print("="*60)
        print("๐ก ููููู ุงูุทูุจ ุจุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ ุฃู ุงูุฅูุฌููุฒูุฉ")
        print("๐ก You can request in Arabic or English")
        print("๐ ุงูุชุจ 'exit' ุฃู 'ุฎุฑูุฌ' ููุฅููุงุก")
        print("๐ Type 'exit' or 'ุฎุฑูุฌ' to quit")
        print("="*60)
        
        # Main interaction loop
        while True:
            try:
                user_input = input("\n๐ฑ ููู ูููููู ูุณุงุนุฏุชูุ How can I help you? ").strip()
                
                if user_input.lower() in ['exit', 'quit', 'ุฎุฑูุฌ', 'ุฅููุงุก']:
                    print("๐ ุดูุฑุงู ูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงููุณุงุนุฏ! Thank you for using the AI Agent!")
                    break
                
                if not user_input:
                    continue
                
                print("\n๐ค ุฌุงุฑู ุงููุนุงูุฌุฉ... Processing...")
                response = agent.invoke({"input": user_input})
                print(f"\nโ {response['output']}")
                
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                print("\n๐ ุชู ุฅููุงู ุงููุณุงุนุฏ. Agent stopped.")
                break
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"\nโ ุฎุทุฃ: {str(e)}")
                print(f"โ Error: {str(e)}")
    
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"โ ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุณุงุนุฏ: {str(e)}")
        print(f"โ Error creating agent: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

                    </div>

            <!-- ููุทูุฉ ุงููุชุงุจุฉ -->
            <div class="p-6 bg-black/20">
                <div class="relative flex items-center glass-panel rounded-2xl p-2">
                    <textarea id="inputField" rows="1" class="w-full bg-transparent border-none focus:ring-0 text-white px-4 py-3 resize-none max-h-32 placeholder-gray-500" placeholder="ุงูุชุจ ุฃูุงูุฑู ููุง..."></textarea>
                    <button onclick="sendMessage()" id="sendBtn" class="p-4 bg-cyan-600 hover:bg-cyan-500 rounded-xl transition shadow-lg shadow-cyan-600/20 ml-2">
                        <i data-lucide="send" class="text-white"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        lucide.createIcons();
        
        let currentModel = "xi_legend:latest";
        const OLLAMA_URL = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate";
        const chatBox = document.getElementById('chatBox');
        const inputField = document.getElementById('inputField');

        // ุฏุงูุฉ ุงูุฅุฑุณุงู
        async function sendMessage() {
            const text = inputField.value.trim();
            if (!text) return;

            // ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู
            appendMessage(text, 'user');
            inputField.value = '';
            inputField.style.height = 'auto';

            // ุฅุถุงูุฉ ูุคุดุฑ ุงูุชุญููู
            const loadingId = showLoading();

            try {
                const response = await fetch(OLLAMA_URL, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        model: currentModel,
                        prompt: `ุฃูุช ูุณุงุนุฏ ุฐูู ููุนุฑูุงุจ 777. ุฃุฌุจ ุจุงุฎุชุตุงุฑ ูุญููุฉ ูุฏูุฉ.\n\nุงูุณุคุงู: ${text}\nุงูุฌูุงุจ:`,
                        stream: false
                    })
                });

                const data = await response.json();
                removeLoading(loadingId);
                
                if (data.response) {
                    appendMessage(data.response, 'ai');
                } else {
                    appendMessage("ุญุฏุซ ุฎุทุฃ ุบูุฑ ูุชููุน ูู ุงููููุฐุฌ ุงููุญูู.", 'ai');
                }

            } catch (error) {
                removeLoading(loadingId);
                appendMessage("โ๏ธ ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุงุชุตุงู! ุชุฃูุฏ ูู ุชุดุบูู 'ollama serve' ูู ุงูุชูุฑูููุงู.", 'ai');
                console.error(error);
            }
        }

        // ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู
        function appendMessage(text, sender) {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.className = `flex ${sender === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`;
            
            // ุชูุณูู ุงููุต (ุชุญููู ุงูุฃุณุทุฑ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ุฅูู <br>)
            const formattedText = text.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');

            div.innerHTML = `
                <div class="${sender === 'user' ? 'message-user' : 'message-ai'} px-6 py-4 max-w-[80%] text-sm md:text-base leading-relaxed">
                    ${formattedText}
                </div>
            `;
            chatBox.appendChild(div);
            chatBox.scrollTop = chatBox.scrollHeight;
        }

        function showLoading() {
            const id = 'loading-' + Date.now();
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.id = id;
            div.className = 'flex justify-start';
            div.innerHTML = `
                <div class="message-ai px-6 py-4">
                    <div class="flex gap-1">
                        <div class="typing-dot"></div>
                        <div class="typing-dot"></div>
                        <div class="typing-dot"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            chatBox.appendChild(div);
            chatBox.scrollTop = chatBox.scrollHeight;
            return id;
        }

        function removeLoading(id) {
            const el = document.getElementById(id);
            if (el) el.remove();
        }

        function setModel(model) {
            currentModel = model;
            document.getElementById('currentModelDisplay').innerText = `ุงูุนูู ุงููุชุตู: ${model}`;
            alert(`ุชู ุงูุชุจุฏูู ุฅูู ุงููููุฐุฌ: ${model}`);
        }

        function clearChat() {
            chatBox.innerHTML = '';
            appendMessage("ุชู ูุณุญ ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุคูุชุฉ. ุงููุธุงู ุฌุงูุฒ.", 'ai');
        }

        // ุฅุฑุณุงู ุนูุฏ ุงูุถุบุท ุนูู Enter
        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                e.preventDefault();
                sendMessage();
            }
            // ุชูุจูุฑ ุงูุญูู ุชููุงุฆูุงู
            e.target.style.height = 'auto';
            e.target.style.height = e.target.scrollHeight + 'px';
        });

    </script>
</body>
</html>
