      const DEFAULT_PHONE = "201234567890"; // ุถุน ุฑููู ุงูุฏููู ุจุฏูู +

      // ูุถุน ุงูุฌููุฉ: ุฑูุญุงููุฉ (ุฃุฒุฑู) / ูุบุงูุฑุฉ (ุฃุญูุฑ)
      const root = document.documentElement;
      const knob = document.getElementById('knob');
      const btnBlue = document.getElementById('modeBlue');
      const btnRed = document.getElementById('modeRed');

      function setMode(mode){
        if(mode === 'blue'){
          root.style.setProperty('--brand-active', getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue('--brand'));
          btnBlue.classList.add('active'); btnRed.classList.remove('active');
          knob.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
          document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]').setAttribute('content','#0ea5e9');
        } else {
          root.style.setProperty('--brand-active', getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue('--brand-2'));
          btnRed.classList.add('active'); btnBlue.classList.remove('active');
          knob.style.transform = 'translateX(100%)';
          document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]').setAttribute('content','#ef4444');
        }
        // ุชุญุฏูุซ QR ุจุฑุงุจุท ุงููุถุน ุงูุญุงูู
        updateQR();
      }

      btnBlue.addEventListener('click', ()=> setMode('blue'));
      btnRed .addEventListener('click', ()=> setMode('red'));

      // === ุชูููุฏ ุฑุงุจุท ูุงุชุณุงุจ ููุนุจูุฃ ===
      function buildWA({offer="General", modeLabel, phone=DEFAULT_PHONE}){
        const text = encodeURIComponent(
          `ูุฑุญุจูุงุ ุฃูุฏ ุงูุญุฌุฒ ูุฌููุฉ ุงูุฃูุฑุงูุงุช โ ูุฒูุฉ ุงูุณูุงู.\nุงูุงุฎุชูุงุฑ: ${offer}.\nุฑูุญ ุงูุฌููุฉ: ${modeLabel}.\nุงูุงุณู: ____\nุงูุชุงุฑูุฎ: ____\nุนุฏุฏ ุงูุฃุดุฎุงุต: ____\nุงุณุชูุณุงุฑุงุช ุฅุถุงููุฉ: ____`
        );
        return `https://wa.me/${phone}?text=${text}`;
      }

      function currentModeLabel(){
        return btnBlue.classList.contains('active') ? 'ุฑูุญุงููุฉ (ุงูุฃุฒุฑู)' : 'ูุบุงูุฑุฉ (ุงูุฃุญูุฑ)';
      }

      const waTop = document.getElementById('waTop');
      const bookPrimary = document.getElementById('bookPrimary');
      const chatAI = document.getElementById('chatAI');

      function updateLinks(){
        const url = buildWA({offer:'ุงุณุชูุณุงุฑ ุนุงู', modeLabel: currentModeLabel()});
        waTop.href = url;
        bookPrimary.href = url;
        chatAI.href = url; // ูููู ูุงุญููุง ุฑุจุทู ุจูุณุงุนุฏ AI ูุนูู ุนุจุฑ ูุงุชุณุงุจ ุจุฒูุณ
      }

      // ุฃุฒุฑุงุฑ ุงูุญุฌุฒ ููู ุนุฑุถ
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-offer]').forEach(a=>{
        a.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
          e.preventDefault();
          const offer = e.currentTarget.dataset.offer;
          const url = buildWA({offer, modeLabel: currentModeLabel()});
          window.open(url, '_blank');
        })
      })

      // === QR ===
      let qr;
      function updateQR(){
        const url = buildWA({offer:'QR Booking', modeLabel: currentModeLabel()});
        const qrBox = document.getElementById('qrcode');
        qrBox.innerHTML = '';
        qr = new QRCode(qrBox, {text:url, width:130, height:130, correctLevel: QRCode.CorrectLevel.M});
      }

      // ูุณุฎ ุฑุงุจุท
      document.getElementById('copyLink').addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        e.preventDefault();
        const url = buildWA({offer:'ุงุณุชูุณุงุฑ ุนุงู', modeLabel: currentModeLabel()});
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(()=>{
          e.currentTarget.textContent = 'ุชู ุงููุณุฎ โ';
          setTimeout(()=> e.currentTarget.textContent='ูุณุฎ ุฑุงุจุท ุงูุญุฌุฒ', 1800);
        });
      });

      // ูุดุงุฑูุฉ ุงููุธุงููุฉ

        const url = buildWA({offer:'ุงุณุชูุณุงุฑ ุนุงู', modeLabel: currentModeLabel()});

        } else {
          window.open(url, '_blank');
        }
      });

      // ูุคุซุฑ ูุฌูู ุจุณูุท ูุชุจุน ุงููุงูุณ
      const stars = document.getElementById('stars');
      const pool = Array.from({length: 30}).map(()=>{
        const s = document.createElement('span');
        s.style.left = Math.random()*100 + 'vw';
        s.style.top = Math.random()*100 + 'vh';

      });
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e)=>{
        const x = e.clientX, y = e.clientY;
        pool.forEach((s,i)=>{
          const d = (i%5)+1; // ุฏุฑุฌุงุช ูุฎุชููุฉ
          s.style.transform = `translate(${(x/window.innerWidth - .5)*d*8}px, ${(y/window.innerHeight - .5)*d*8}px)`;
        })
      });

   - ูู ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ูุฌุจ ุฃู ุชููุชุจ ุชุญุช ุนููุงู ูุงุถุญุ ูุน ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุฅู ุฃููู.

**4. ููู ุงูุณูุงู ูุชุฌูุจ ุฃุฎุทุงุก ุงูุฅุฏุฎุงู - ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ**
   - **ุญุฑุต ุดุฏูุฏ ุนูู ุณูุงู ุงูุญุฏูุซ:** ูุฌุจ ุงูุงูุชุจุงู ุฅูู ุณูุงู ุงูุญุฏูุซ ุงูุนุงู ูุงููุญูุฑ ุงูุฃุณุงุณู ูููุดุฑูุน (ูุงุฐุง ูุชููู ุนููุ ุฃูู ุฐุงูุจููุ ูุง ูู ุงููุฏู ุงูุฃุณุงุณู).
   - **ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุฃูุฏุงู:** ุฃู ุดูุก ุฌุงูุจู ูุฌุจ ุฃู ูููู ูุชุญููู ุงููุฏู ุงูุฃุณุงุณู. ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ุบูุฑ ุฐููุ ูุฌุจ ุงูุณุคุงู ูุจู ุงุชุฎุงุฐ ุฃู ูุฑุงุฑ ุฃู ูุณุงุฑ ูุงูู.
   - **ุงูุชุนุงูู ูุน ุฃุฎุทุงุก ููุญุฉ ุงูููุงุชูุญ:** ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก ุงูุฅููุงุฆูุฉ ุฃู ุงููุบููุฉ ุงููุงุชุฌุฉ ุนู ุฃุฎุทุงุก ููุญุฉ ุงูููุงุชูุญ ูุฌุจ ุฃูุง ุชุคุฏู ุฅูู ุชุบููุฑ ููุญูู ูุงูู ูู ุงููุณุงุฑ. ุชูููู ุงููููุฉ ูู ุณูุงููุง ุงูุฃูุณุน ูุชุฌูุจ ุณูุก ุงูุชูุณูุฑ ูุชุบููุฑ ุงูููุฉ.

---
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
๐ฑ Super Power AI Agent
ูููู ุฎุงุฑู ูุชุนุฏุฏ ุงููุฏุฑุงุชุ ุฌุงูุฒ ููุชุทููุฑ ุงููุชุณูุณู
"""

import os, sys, subprocess
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv

# LangChain imports
from langchain_openai import ChatOpenAI
from langchain_community.llms import Ollama
from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
from langchain.memory import ConversationBufferWindowMemory
from langchain.agents import AgentExecutor, create_react_agent
from langchain.tools import BaseTool

# ุชุญููู ูุชุบูุฑุงุช ุงูุจูุฆุฉ
load_dotenv(Path.home() / ".env")

# =========================
# ๐๏ธ ุงูุฃุฏูุงุช (Tools)
# =========================

class SystemCommandTool(BaseTool):
    """๐ง ุฃุฏุงุฉ ูุชูููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงููุธุงู ุจุฃูุงู"""
    name = "system_command"
    description = "Execute system commands safely"

    def _run(self, command: str) -> str:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(command, shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)
            return f"Exit Code: {result.returncode}\nOutput:\n{result.stdout}\nError:\n{result.stderr}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error executing command: {str(e)}"

    async def _arun(self, command: str) -> str:
        return self._run(command)

class FileOperationsTool(BaseTool):
    """๐ ุฃุฏุงุฉ ูุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงููููุงุช (ูุฑุงุกุฉ/ูุชุงุจุฉ/ูุงุฆูุฉ)"""
    name = "file_operations"
    description = "Manage files on the system"

    def _run(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        path = Path(file_path).expanduser().resolve()
        try:
            if operation == "read":
                return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8") if path.exists() else f"File {file_path} not found"
            elif operation == "write":
                path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
                return f"Written to {file_path}"
            elif operation == "append":
                with path.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(content)
                return f"Appended to {file_path}"
            elif operation == "list":
                return "\n".join([str(f) for f in path.iterdir()]) if path.is_dir() else f"{file_path} not a directory"
            else:
                return f"Unknown operation: {operation}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"File operation error: {str(e)}"

    async def _arun(self, operation: str, file_path: str, content: str = "") -> str:
        return self._run(operation, file_path, content)

class PythonCodeTool(BaseTool):
    """๐ ุฃุฏุงุฉ ูุชูููุฐ ููุฏ ุจุงูุซูู ุจุฃูุงู"""
    name = "python_code"
    description = "Execute Python code safely"

    def _run(self, code: str) -> str:
        try:
            exec_globals = {"__builtins__": __builtins__, "os": os, "sys": sys, "Path": Path}
            from io import StringIO
            old_stdout = sys.stdout
            sys.stdout = captured_output = StringIO()
            exec(code, exec_globals)
            sys.stdout = old_stdout
            return captured_output.getvalue() or "Code executed successfully"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Python execution error: {str(e)}"

    async def _arun(self, code: str) -> str:
        return self._run(code)

# =========================
# โก ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููููู
# =========================

def create_agent():
    # ุงุฎุชูุงุฑ ุงููููุฐุฌ: Ollama ุฃู OpenAI
    if os.getenv("USE_OLLAMA", "false").lower() == "true":
        llm = Ollama(model=os.getenv("OLLAMA_MODEL", "llama3:2"))
    else:
        llm = ChatOpenAI(
            model=os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "gpt-4o"),
            temperature=0.7,
            openai_api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        )

    # ุฐุงูุฑุฉ ูุดุชุฑูุฉ (ูููู ุฑุจุทูุง ุจููู ุฃู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุจูุงูุงุช)
    memory = ConversationBufferWindowMemory(memory_key="chat_history", k=20, return_messages=True)

    # ูุงูุจ ุงูุชุนูููุงุช
    prompt = PromptTemplate.from_template("""
ุฃูุช ูููู ุฎุงุฑู ูุชุนุฏุฏ ุงููุฏุฑุงุช:
- ุชููุฐ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงููุธุงู
- ุชุฏูุฑ ุงููููุงุช
- ุชุดุบูู ููุฏ ุจุงูุซูู
- ุชุฑุฏ ุจุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ ุฃู ุงูุฅูุฌููุฒูุฉ ุญุณุจ ูุบุฉ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู
- ุชุญูุธ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ ูู ุฐุงูุฑุฉ ูุดุชุฑูุฉ

ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ:
{chat_history}

ุงูุณุคุงู: {input}
{agent_scratchpad}
""")

    # ุงูุฃุฏูุงุช ุงููุถุงูุฉ
    tools = [SystemCommandTool(), FileOperationsTool(), PythonCodeTool()]

    agent = create_react_agent(llm, tools, prompt)
    return AgentExecutor(agent=agent, tools=tools, memory=memory, verbose=True)

# =========================
# ๐ ุงูุชุดุบูู
# =========================

def main():
    print("๐ฑ Super Power Agent Ready")
    agent = create_agent()
    while True:
        user_input = input("\n๐ก ุฃุฏุฎู ุทูุจู: ").strip()
        if user_input.lower() in ["exit", "quit", "ุฎุฑูุฌ"]:
            print("๐ ุงูุชูุช ุงูุฌูุณุฉ")
            break
        response = agent.invoke({"input": user_input})
        print(f"\nโ {response['output']}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()



*ููุงูุฉ ุงูุฅุตุฏุงุฑ 0.2 ูู Box777.md โ ุฎุงุต ุจุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ููุท. (ุชุงุฑูุฎ: 2025-11-23)*






# Pinokio

Launch Anything.

# Script Policy
w
Pinokio is a 1-click launcher for any open-source project. Think of it as a terminal application with a user-friendly interface that can programmatically interact with scripts.

This means:

1. **Scripts can run anything:** Just like terminal apps can run shell scripts, Pinokio scripts can run any command, download files, and execute them. Essentially, Pinokio is a user-friendly terminal with a UI.
2. **How scripts can be run:** There are two ways to run scripts on Pinokio:
    1. **Write your own:** Just like writing and executing shell scripts in the terminal, you can create your own scripts and run them locally.
    2. **Install from the "Discover" page:** Vetted scripts are manually listed in the directory, tracked via Git, and frozen under the official GitHub organization. These are guaranteed to be secure and safe to install.
3. **Verified Scripts:** To be featured on the "Discover" page, scripts must go through the following strict process:
    1. **Publisher Verification:** You must be personally verified to submit scripts for consideration. Contact the Pinokio admin (https://x.com/cocktailpeanut) to request verification.
    2. **Github Organization Invitation:** Once verified, you'll be invited to the official Pinokio Factory GitHub organization as a contributor. Only members of this organization can publish scripts eligible for the "Discover" page. Abusing publishing privileges may result in removal from the organization.
    3. **Repository Transfer and Freeze** To apply for a feature, you must transfer your script repository to the Pinokio Factory GitHub organization. Follow this guide: https://docs.github.com/en/repositories/creating-and-managing-repositories/transferring-a-repository
    4. **Feature Application:** Once your repository is fully transferred and controlled by the organization, it is considered "frozen". You can then request to feature it on the "Discover" page by contacting the admin.
    5. **Review:** The script will be thoroughly reviewed and tested by the Pinokio admin. If verified as safe, it will be featured on the "Discover" page.
    6. **Troubleshooting:** If any issues arise after a script is featured, the Pinokio admin may:
        - Delist the script from the "Discover" page
        - Modify the script to resolve the issue. Since the script is under the Pinokio Factory organization, the admin has the rights to make necessary fixes.

# Security

## Scripts are isolated by design

By default all Pinokio scripts are stored run under an isolated location (at `~/pinokio/api`). Additionally, all binaries installed through the built-in package managers in Pinokio are installed within `~/pinokio/bin`. Basically, everything you do is stored inside `~/pinokio`. The risk factor is when a script intentionally tries to deviatte away from this.

The script verification process checks to make sure this doesn't happen.

Th Pinokio script syntax was designed to make this process simpler, both by human and machines.

## Scripts are open source

All scripts must be downloaded from public git repositories. The scripts are both human readable and machine readable (written in JSON syntax), so you can always check the source code before running it.

Here's an example install screen, with an alert letting you know the downloaded 3rd party script is about to be run, as well as the URL to the original script repository where it was downloaded from.

![install.png](install.png)

## Script Verification

Verified scripts are scripts that are explicitly reviewed and approved by the Pinokio admin. Because the scripts are designed to run isolated by default, and the syntax makes it easy to detect when a command intentionally tries to run things outside of the isolated environment, it is easy to detect any script that does things out of the ordinary. Here are some of the checks done by the Pinokio admin to make sure each script file is secure:

1. **Path check:** When we verify the scripts, we look at the scripts to see if all commands are run inside each app's path. The script syntax was designed to make this process easy (with the `path` attribute, which declares the folder path from which to run a command, and by default the execution path is each app's path)
2. **Venv check:** We also check to make sure every dependency installation is done within the context of each app using `venv`. This process is again made easy with the script syntax (with the `venv` attribute, which automatically activates a virtual environment and installs all dependencies there, inside each app's folder)
3. **3rd Party Package check:** We also check that any 3rd party packages installed through Pinokio to make sure that they are installed inside the pinokio isolated environment. The built-in package mangagers (Conda, Homebrew, Pip, and NPM) install everything inside the isolated pinokio home path (`~/pinokio`) by default. Since everything runs isolated by default, verifying this is simple (by checking that there are no explicit declaration of additional code that tries to go outside of the isolated environment)

Here's an example execution script that installs python dependencies:

```json
{
  "method": "shell.run",
  "params": {
    "message": "uv pip install -r requirements.txt",
    "path": "server",
    "venv": "venv"
  }
}
```

1. First of all, by default the entire thing is run isolated in the pinokio activated conda environment, and the execution path is the downloaded apwwwwp's path (for example `w`)
2. second, since the `path` is declared as `server`, the code will be run inside the `server` folder ofr the app (in this case `~/pinokio/api/myapp/server`)
3. Third, the `venv` attribute  is included, so the python dependencies are also installed in an app-isolated manner. If the app is located at `~/pinokio/api/myapp`, the The depenencies will be stored at `~/pinokio/api/myapp/venv`

The script verification check makes sure that all these components are run locally within the constraints of each app.

Of course, there are also additional checks such as:

1. Checking the reputation of the repository and the developer of the original project
2. Trhing out the app personally
3. Making sure that the install and launch instructions actually follow the recommended instructions suggested in the original project's README.

B_777_#!/bin/zsh
# ==========================================
# ๐ง AlArab Advance Agent (One-Click Launch)
# by AlArab777
# ==========================================

PROJECT_DIR="$HOME/AlArab777"
AGENT_PY="$PROJECT_DIR/advanced-ai-agent.py"
HTTP_PORT=3000
LM_STUDIO_APP_NAME="LM Studio"
LM_API_HOST="127.0.0.1"
LM_API_PORT=1234
LOG_DIR="/tmp/alarab_advance"
HTTP_LOG="$LOG_DIR/http.log"
LM_LOG="$LOG_DIR/lm_studio.log"
AGENT_LOG="$LOG_DIR/agent.log"
PID_DIR="/tmp/alarab_pids"

mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR" "$PID_DIR"
clear

log() { echo "[$(date '+%H:%M:%S')] $*"; echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] $*" >>"$LOG_DIR/advance_agent.log"; }

cd "$PROJECT_DIR" || { log "โ ุงููุดุฑูุน ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ: $PROJECT_DIR"; exit 1; }

# ุชุญููู ููู ุงูุจูุฆุฉ ุฅู ูุฌุฏ
[ -f .env ] && source .env 2>/dev/null

log "๐ ุชุดุบูู AlArab Advance Agent ..."

# --- ุชุดุบูู LM Studio ---
if ! pgrep -f "LM Studio" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  log "๐ง ูุชุญ LM Studio ..."
  open -a "$LM_STUDIO_APP_NAME" >/dev/null 2>&1 &
  sleep 6
else
  log "โน๏ธ LM Studio ูุนูู ูุณุจููุง"
fi

# ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฃู ุงูู API ูุนูู
for i in {1..12}; do
  if curl --silent "http://$LM_API_HOST:$LM_API_PORT/v1/models" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "โ LM Studio API ุฌุงูุฒ ุนูู http://$LM_API_HOST:$LM_API_PORT"
    break
  fi
  log "โฆ ุงูุชุธุงุฑ LM Studio ($i/12)"
  sleep 1
done

# --- ุชุดุบูู ุงูุณูุฑูุฑ ุงููุญูู (ุจุฏูู ุนุฑุถ ูุญุชูู ุงููุฌูุฏ) ---
if ! lsof -iTCP:"$HTTP_PORT" -sTCP:LISTEN >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  log "๐ ุจุฏุก python http.server ุนูู ุงููููุฐ $HTTP_PORT ..."
  nohup python3 -m http.server "$HTTP_PORT" --bind 0.0.0.0 >"$HTTP_LOG" 2>&1 &
  echo $! > "$PID_DIR/http.pid"
else
  log "โ๏ธ ุงููููุฐ $HTTP_PORT ูุณุชุฎุฏู โ ุชุฎุทูู ุชุดุบูู ุงูุณูุฑูุฑ"

# --- ุชุดุบูู ููู ุงููููู ---

1) ููู NOAH-AutoNode.js (MVP)

ุงูููู ุงูุชุงูู ูุนุทูู ูุธุงู ุชุดุบูู ุฃูุชููุงุชููู Agent Loop ูุน

ุงูุณุฎู ูุงูู ูุงุญูุธู ุจุงุณู:

/Users/macos/AlArab777/NOAH_AutoNode.js

/* ==================  NOAH-AutoNode.js  (MVP)  ==================
   Server = 3000 + 7777
   Memory = M3 Full Autonomous
   Sheet = Google Sheet Live Sync
   OS 777 โ Multi-Agent ยท Voice ยท LLM Local ยท Task-Chain Recursive
=================================================================*/

import express from "express";
import bodyParser from "body-parser";
import axios from "axios";
import { GoogleSpreadsheet } from "google-spreadsheet";
import { exec } from "child_process";

/*============================ CONFIG ============================*/
const PORT_MAIN = 3000;        // Web UI API
const PORT_AGENT = 7777;       // Agent Loop Exec
const SHEET_URL = "https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/e/2PACX-1vTJTjrc2XpvaRgS9B11fP4vqYGRUh2umAvZOko79A17Vdc8xlyHr4mJ_QIUQsLFYKvV0E46mg-ChJvf";

const LLM_ENDPOINT = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate"; // Ollama API
const MODEL = "llama3"; // ููููู ุชุบููุฑูุง ูู qwen/mixtral

/*============================ SHEETS ============================*/
async function writeToSheet(task, agent, status="Active", result="", progress="0%") {
    // Minimal Sheet Engine (will be extended)
    console.log(`[SHEET] Logging:`, task);
    // ูุงุญูุงู ูุฑุจุท Auth + Write API ุจุดูู ูุงูู
}

/*============================ CORE LOOP ============================*/
async function runAgentTask(inputText, agent="master") {

    const payload = {
        model: MODEL,
        prompt: `Agent:${agent}\nTask:${inputText}\nOutput ONLY result.\n`
    };

    const response = await axios.post(LLM_ENDPOINT, payload, { responseType:"json" });
    const result = response.data.output || response.data;
    
    await writeToSheet(inputText, agent, "Done", result);
    return result;
}

/*============================ EXPRESS APIs ============================*/
const app = express();
app.use(bodyParser.json());

app.post("/ask", async (req,res)=>{
    const { text, agent="master" } = req.body;
    const out = await runAgentTask(text, agent);
    res.send({reply:out});
});

app.get("/",(req,res)=> res.send("NOAH-AutoNode.js 777 Running"));

/*============================ AUTO LOOP ============================*/
function autoLoop(){
    console.log(`โ Noah Loop Started โ Auto Execution`);
    // ูุงุญูุงู: ููุฑุฃ Queue ูู Sheet โ ูุณุชุฏุนู runAgentTask โ ูููุฏ Sub-Tasks ูุซู ุดุฌุฑุฉ
}

app.listen(PORT_MAIN, ()=> console.log(`MAIN API on :${PORT_MAIN}`));
autoLoop();

/*  ุชุดุบูู ูููุตู ูููููู ุฎููู ุนูู 7777  */
exec(`node NOAH_AutoNode.js --agent`,()=>{});
console.log(`AGENT LOOP on :${PORT_AGENT}`);


โธป

2) ุณูุฑูุจุช ุชุดุบูู ุดุงูู ููุฑู

ุงูุณุฎู ูููู ุชุดุบูู ุจุงุณู:

start_777.sh

#!/bin/bash
echo "๐ Starting 777 NOAH Intelligence Stackโฆ"

cd /Users/macos/AlArab777

# Local LLM
ollama serve &

# Agent Auto Node
node NOAH_AutoNode.js &

echo "Done โ  API โ http://localhost:3000"
echo "Done โ  AgentLoop โ http://localhost:7777"

ุชุดุบููู:

chmod +x start_777.sh
./start_777.sh


โธป

3) ุทุฑููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูุขู (ุจุฏูู ููุงู)

ุฃูุชุจ ูู Pinokio Terminal ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ:

node NOAH_AutoNode.js

ุฃู ูู Postman / CURL:

curl -X POST http://localhost:3000/ask -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-d '{"text":"ุญูู ุฎุทุฉ 777","agent":"master"}'

ุงููุชูุฌุฉ ูุธูุฑ + ูุชู ุชุณุฌูููุง ูู ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ Sheets.

โธป

def get_reference_audio():
    wavs_dir = MODEL_PATH / "wavs"
    
    # ุงุณุชุฎุฏู ููู ูุญุฏุฏ ุจุฏูุงู ูู ุนุดูุงุฆู
    selected = wavs_dir / "audio_005.wav"  # ูุซูุงู
    
    return selected

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { Send, Users, MessageCircle, Loader2, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';

const AgentsChatRoom = () => {
  const [agents, setAgents] = useState([
    { id: 1, name: 'ุงููุญูู', role: 'ุชุญููู ุงูุฃููุงุฑ ูุงูุจูุงูุงุช', color: 'bg-blue-500' },
    { id: 2, name: 'ุงููุจุฏุน', role: 'ุงูุฃููุงุฑ ุงูุฅุจุฏุงุนูุฉ ูุงูุญููู', color: 'bg-purple-500' },
    { id: 3, name: 'ุงููุงูุฏ', role: 'ุชูููู ูููุฏ ุงูุฃููุงุฑ', color: 'bg-red-500' },
  ]);
  
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
  const [currentInput, setCurrentInput] = useState('');
  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);
  const [currentAgentIndex, setCurrentAgentIndex] = useState(-1);
  const messagesEndRef = useRef(null);

  const scrollToBottom = () => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    scrollToBottom();
  }, [messages]);

  const addAgent = () => {
    const newAgent = {
      id: agents.length + 1,
    
      name: `ูููู ${agents.length + 1}`,
      role: 'ุฏูุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏ',
      color: `bg-${['green', 'yellow', 'pink', 'indigo', 'orange'][agents.length % 5]}-500`
    };
    setAgents([...agents, newAgent]);
  };

  const removeAgent = (id) => {
    if (agents.length > 1) {
      setAgents(agents.filter(a => a.id !== id));
    }
  };

  const callClaudeAPI = async (prompt, agentContext) => {
    try {
      const conversationHistory = messages.map(msg => ({
        role: msg.isUser ? 'user' : 'assistant',
        content: msg.text
      }));

      const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/json",
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          model: "claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
          max_tokens: 2000,
          messages: [
            ...conversationHistory,
            {
              role: "user",
              content: `ุฃูุช ${agentContext.name} - ${agentContext.role}.

ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉ ุงููุงููุฉ ุญุชู ุงูุขู:
${messages.map(m => `${m.agent || 'ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู'}: ${m.text}`).join('\n')}

ุงูุขู ุฏูุฑู ููุฑุฏ. ููููู:
- ุงูุฑุฏ ุนูู ุงูููุงุท ุงููุทุฑูุญุฉ
- ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฃููุงุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ุจูุงุกู ุนูู ุฏูุฑู
- ุงูุชูุงุนู ูุน ูุง ูุงูู ุงูุขุฎุฑูู

ุฑุฏ ุจุดูู ููุฌุฒ ููููุฏ (2-4 ุฌูู):

${prompt}`
            }
          ]
        })
      });

      const data = await response.json();
      return data.content[0].text;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error calling Claude:', error);
      return 'ุนุฐุฑุงูุ ุญุฏุซ ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุงุชุตุงู.';
    }
  };

  const startDiscussion = async () => {
    if (!currentInput.trim() || isProcessing) return;

    const userMessage = {
      id: Date.now(),
      text: currentInput,
      agent: 'ุฃูุช',
      isUser: true,
      color: 'bg-gray-700'
    };

    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMessage]);
    setCurrentInput('');
    setIsProcessing(true);

    // ุงูุฏูุฑุฉ ุชุจุฏุฃ ูู ุฃูู ูููู
    for (let i = 0; i < agents.length; i++) {
      setCurrentAgentIndex(i);
      
      const agent = agents[i];
      const agentResponse = await callClaudeAPI(currentInput, agent);
      
      const agentMessage = {
        id: Date.now() + i,
        text: agentResponse,
        agent: agent.name,
        color: agent.color,
        isUser: false
      };
      
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, agentMessage]);
      
      // ุชููู ูุตูุฑ ุจูู ุงููููุงุก
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
    }

    setCurrentAgentIndex(-1);
    setIsProcessing(false);
  };

  const handleKeyPress = (e) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
      e.preventDefault();
      startDiscussion();
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-gray-900 via-gray-800 to-gray-900 text-white p-4" dir="rtl">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg p-6 mb-4 shadow-xl">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <Users className="w-8 h-8 text-blue-400" />
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">ุบุฑูุฉ ุงููููุงุก ุงูุฑูููุฉ</h1>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={addAgent}
              className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg transition"
            >
              <Plus className="w-5 h-5" />
              ุฅุถุงูุฉ ูููู
            </button>
          </div>
          
          {/* Agents Display */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-3">
            {agents.map((agent, index) => (
              <div 
                key={agent.id} 
                className={`${agent.color} ${currentAgentIndex === index ? 'ring-4 ring-yellow-400 scale-105' : ''} bg-opacity-20 border-2 ${agent.color.replace('bg-', 'border-')} rounded-lg p-4 transition-all duration-300`}
              >
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-full ${agent.color} ${currentAgentIndex === index ? 'animate-pulse' : ''}`}></div>
                    <h3 className="font-bold text-lg">{agent.name}</h3>
                  </div>
                  {agents.length > 1 && (
                    <button
                      onClick={() => removeAgent(agent.id)}
                      className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 transition"
                    >
                      <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-300">{agent.role}</p>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Chat Area */}
        <div className="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl flex flex-col h-[600px]">
          {/* Messages */}
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
            {messages.length === 0 && (
              <div className="text-center text-gray-400 mt-20">
                <MessageCircle className="w-16 h-16 mx-auto mb-4 opacity-50" />
                <p className="text-xl">ุงุจุฏุฃ ุงูููุงุด ูุดุงูุฏ ุงููููุงุก ูุชูุงุนููู!</p>
              </div>
            )}
            
            {messages.map((message) => (
              <div
                key={message.id}
                className={`flex ${message.isUser ? 'justify-start' : 'justify-end'}`}
              >
                <div className={`max-w-[80%] ${message.color} bg-opacity-20 border-2 ${message.color.replace('bg-', 'border-')} rounded-lg p-4`}>
                  <div className="font-bold text-sm mb-1 opacity-90">{message.agent}</div>
                  <div className="text-white leading-relaxed">{message.text}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
            
            {isProcessing && (
              <div className="flex justify-center">
                <div className="bg-blue-500 bg-opacity-20 border-2 border-blue-500 rounded-lg p-4 flex items-center gap-3">
                  <Loader2 className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin" />
                  <span>ุงููููุงุก ูููุฑูู...</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
            
            <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
          </div>

          {/* Input Area */}
          <div className="border-t border-gray-700 p-4">
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={currentInput}
                onChange={(e) => setCurrentInput(e.target.value)}
                onKeyPress={handleKeyPress}
                placeholder="ุงูุชุจ ุณุคุงูู ุฃู ููุถูุนู ููููุงุด..."
                disabled={isProcessing}
                className="flex-1 bg-gray-700 text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 disabled:opacity-50"
              />
              <button
                onClick={startDiscussion}
                disabled={isProcessing || !currentInput.trim()}
                className="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 disabled:bg-gray-600 disabled:cursor-not-allowed px-6 py-3 rounded-lg transition flex items-center gap-2"
              >
                <Send className="w-5 h-5" />
                ุฅุฑุณุงู
              </button>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-2 text-center">
              ุณูุฑุฏ ูู ูููู ุจุฏูุฑู ุนูู ููุถูุนู ุจูุงุกู ุนูู ุชุฎุตุตู
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AgentsChatRoom;

            ูู ุจุทุงูุฉ ุชูุซู ูููู ูุณุชููุ ุงูุฑุฏูุฏ ุชุธูุฑ ูู ููุทูู ุงูุฎุงุตุฉ.

  <script>
    // ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงููููุงุก โ ุนุฏูู ุงูุฃุณูุงุก/ุงูุฃุฏูุงุฑ ููุง ุชุญุจ
    const AGENTS = [
      { id: "master", name: "Master777", role: "ุงูุชูุณูู ุงูุนุงู ูุงุฎุชูุงุฑ ุงูุงุณุชุฑุงุชูุฌูุฉ" },
      { id: "expert", name: "Expert777", role: "ุญู ุงููุดููุงุช ุงูุชูููุฉ ูุงูุชูููุฐ ุงูุตุงุฑู" },
      { id: "student", name: "Student777", role: "ุงูุชุนููู ูุงูุดุฑุญ ูุงูุชุจุณูุท" },
      { id: "communicator", name: "Communicator777", role: "ุงูุตูุงุบุฉ ูุงููุชุงุจุฉ ุงูุจุดุฑูุฉ" },
      { id: "archivist", name: "Archivist777", role: "ุงูุฃุฑุดูุฉ ูุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงูุณุฌู" },
      { id: "personal", name: "Personal777", role: "ุชูุธูู ุญูุงุฉ/ููุงู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ" },
      { id: "tourist", name: "Tourist777", role: "ุงูุณูุงุญุฉ ูุงููุญุชูู ุงูููุฏุงูู" }
    ];

    const API_URL = "http://localhost:3000/ask";

    const agentsGrid = document.getElementById("agentsGrid");
    const broadcastInput = document.getElementById("broadcastInput");
    const btnBroadcast = document.getElementById("btnBroadcast");
    const btnClearAll = document.getElementById("btnClearAll");

    const agentState = {}; // ููู ูููู: {messagesDiv, input, sending}

    function appendMessage(agentId, text, type) {
      const state = agentState[agentId];
      if (!state) return;
      const div = document.createElement("div");
      div.classList.add("msg");
      if (type === "user") div.classList.add("msg-user");
      else if (type === "agent") div.classList.add("msg-agent");
      else div.classList.add("msg-system");
      div.textContent = text;
      state.messages.appendChild(div);
      state.messages.scrollTop = state.messages.scrollHeight;
    }

    function setSending(agentId, isSending) {
      const state = agentState[agentId];
      if (!state) return;
      state.sending = isSending;
      state.button.disabled = isSending;
    }

    async function sendToAgent(agentId, text) {
      if (!text.trim()) return;
      const state = agentState[agentId];
      appendMessage(agentId, text, "user");
      setSending(agentId, true);

      try {
        const res = await fetch(API_URL, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ text, agent: agentId })
        });

        if (!res.ok) {
          appendMessage(agentId, "ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุฎุงุฏู (" + res.status + ")", "system");
        } else {
          const data = await res.json();
          const reply = data.reply || data.response || JSON.stringify(data);
          appendMessage(agentId, reply, "agent");
        }
      } catch (err) {
        appendMessage(agentId, "ุชุนุฐุฑ ุงูุงุชุตุงู ุจู localhost:3000", "system");
      } finally {
        setSending(agentId, false);
      }
    }

    function buildAgentCards() {
      AGENTS.forEach(agent => {
        const card = document.createElement("div");
        card.className = "agent-card";

        const header = document.createElement("div");
        header.className = "agent-header";

        const left = document.createElement("div");
        const name = document.createElement("div");
        name.className = "agent-name";
        name.textContent = agent.name;
        const role = document.createElement("div");
        role.className = "agent-role";
        role.textContent = agent.role;
        left.appendChild(name);
        left.appendChild(role);

        const chip = document.createElement("div");
        chip.className = "badge";
        chip.innerHTML = '<span class="status-dot"></span>Online';

        header.appendChild(left);
        header.appendChild(chip);

        const body = document.createElement("div");
        body.className = "agent-body";

        const messages = document.createElement("div");
        messages.className = "messages";
        messages.id = "messages-" + agent.id;
        messages.innerHTML = '<div class="msg msg-system">ุฌุงูุฒ ูุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงูุฃูุงูุฑโฆ</div>';

        const inputRow = document.createElement("div");
        inputRow.className = "agent-input-row";
        const input = document.createElement("input");
        input.type = "text";
        input.placeholder = "ุฃูุฑ ููุฐุง ุงููููู ููุทโฆ";
        const button = document.createElement("button");
        button.textContent = "ุฅุฑุณุงู";

        inputRow.appendChild(input);
        inputRow.appendChild(button);

        body.appendChild(messages);
        body.appendChild(inputRow);

        card.appendChild(header);
        card.appendChild(body);

        agentsGrid.appendChild(card);

        agentState[agent.id] = { messages, input, button, sending: false };

        button.addEventListener("click", () => {
          const txt = input.value;
          input.value = "";
          sendToAgent(agent.id, txt);
        });

        input.addEventListener("keydown", (e) => {
          if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const txt = input.value;
            input.value = "";
            sendToAgent(agent.id, txt);
          }
        });
      });
    }

    buildAgentCards();

    btnBroadcast.addEventListener("click", async () => {
      const text = broadcastInput.value;
      if (!text.trim()) return;
      broadcastInput.value = "";
      AGENTS.forEach(agent => {
        sendToAgent(agent.id, text);
      });
    });

    btnClearAll.addEventListener("click", () => {
      Object.keys(agentState).forEach(id => {
        const s = agentState[id];
        s.messages.innerHTML = '<div class="msg msg-system">ุชู ูุณุญ ุงูุณุฌู. ุฌุงูุฒ ูุฃูุงูุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉโฆ</div>';
      });
    });
  </script>
</body>

function obfuscateCode(code) {
    let output = '';
    const key = KEY.charCodeAt(0);
    
    // ุชุดููู ุงููุญุชูู ุนุจุฑ XOR
    for (let i = 0; i < code.length; i++) {
        output += String.fromCharCode(code.charCodeAt(i) ^ key);

    const base64Encoded = Buffer.from(output, 'binary').toString('base64');

    return `

/* ูุฐุง ุงูููุฏ ูุดููุ ุงูููุงุฌู ุณูุฌุฏ ููุง ุจูุงูุงุช ุบูุฑ ูููููุฉ. */

        originalCode += String.fromCharCode(decoded.charCodeAt(i) ^ K);

    document.close();
} catch (e) {
    document.write('<h1 style="color:red;">โ Mirror Defense Failure: Code Execution Halted.</h1>');
}
    `;
}

// โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ ูุธููุฉ ุงููุนุงูุฌุฉ โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

function processFile() {
    if (!fs.existsSync(ORIGINAL_FILE)) {
        console.error(`โ ูุดู: ุงูููู ุงูุฃุตูู ูููุงุฌูุฉ ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ. ูุฑุฌู ุญูุธู ุจุงุณู: ${path.basename(ORIGINAL_FILE)}`);
        return;
    }

    console.log("๐ ุจุฏุก ูุธุงู ุงููุฑุขุฉ ุงูุฏูุงุนู (Mirror Defense System)...");

    const originalCode = fs.readFileSync(ORIGINAL_FILE, 'utf8');
    const obfuscatedCode = obfuscateCode(originalCode);

    // ูุชุงุจุฉ ุงูููุฏ ุงููุดูู ูููู JavaScript
    fs.writeFileSync(MIRROR_FILE, obfuscatedCode, 'utf8');

    console.log(`โ ุชู ุญูุงูุฉ ุงูููุฏ ูุญูุธ ุงููุณุฎุฉ ุงููุดููุฉ ูู: ${MIRROR_FILE}`);
    console.log(`\n๐ก ูุชุดุบูู ุงููุณุฎุฉ ุงููุญููุฉุ ุงุชุจุน ุงูุฎุทูุงุช ูู ุฏููู README ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ.`);
    console.log("๐ก๏ธ ุชู ุชูุนูู ูุธุงู ุงููุฑุขุฉ. ุงูููุงุฌู ุณูุฌุฏ ุฃููุงุฏ ูุดููุฉ.");

#!/bin/bash
# ========================================================
# ๐ค AlArabClub777 AI Stack Connector
# by ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ุดุฑูู ุงูุดุงููุด
# ========================================================

CYAN="\033[0;36m"
GREEN="\033[0;32m"
YELLOW="\033[1;33m"
RED="\033[0;31m"
RESET="\033[0m"

echo -e "${CYAN}๐น Checking AI Stack connectivity...${RESET}"

# 1๏ธโฃ Check if Ollama is running
if pgrep -x "ollama" > /dev/null; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ Ollama running on localhost:11434${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${YELLOW}โ๏ธ Starting Ollama server...${RESET}"
    nohup ollama serve > /tmp/ollama.log 2>&1 &
    sleep 3
fi

# 2๏ธโฃ Check if VLLM is running
if lsof -Pi :8090 -sTCP:LISTEN -t >/dev/null ; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ VLLM active on port 8090${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${YELLOW}โ๏ธ Starting VLLM (Mistral model)...${RESET}"
    nohup vllm serve mistral --port 8090 > /tmp/vllm.log 2>&1 &
    sleep 5
fi

# 3๏ธโฃ Create Litellm config file
CONFIG_PATH="$HOME/.config/litellm/config.yaml"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$CONFIG_PATH")"

cat > "$CONFIG_PATH" <<EOF
model_list:
  - model_name: local-llama3
    litellm_params:
      model: hosted_vllm/llama3
      api_base: http://localhost:8090

  - model_name: ollama-mistral
    litellm_params:
      model: ollama/mistral
      api_base: http://localhost:11434
EOF

echo -e "${CYAN}๐ Config file created at:${RESET} $CONFIG_PATH"

# 4๏ธโฃ Start Litellm proxy
if lsof -Pi :4000 -sTCP:LISTEN -t >/dev/null ; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ Litellm Proxy already running on port 4000${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${YELLOW}โ๏ธ Launching Litellm Proxy...${RESET}"
    nohup litellm proxy --config "$CONFIG_PATH" > /tmp/litellm.log 2>&1 &
    sleep 5
fi

# 5๏ธโฃ Final connectivity test
echo -e "${CYAN}๐ Testing local endpoints...${RESET}"
if curl -s http://localhost:11434/api/tags >/dev/null; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ Ollama responding properly${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${RED}โ Ollama not responding${RESET}"
fi

if curl -s http://localhost:8090/v1/models >/dev/null; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ VLLM responding properly${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${RED}โ VLLM not responding${RESET}"
fi

if curl -s http://localhost:4000/health >/dev/null; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}โ Litellm proxy is connected${RESET}"
else
    echo -e "${RED}โ Litellm proxy connection failed${RESET}"
fi

echo -e "${CYAN}--------------------------------------------------${RESET}"
echo -e "${GREEN}๐ All systems initialized โ 777 AI Gateway Active${RESET}"
echo -e "${CYAN}--------------------------------------------------${RESET}"

import express from "express";
import fetch from "node-fetch";
import cors from "cors";
import path from "path";
import { fileURLToPath } from "url";

const MODEL = "llama3";
const OLLAMA_API = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate";
const PORT = 7777;

// ุชุญุฏูุฏ ูุฌูุฏ ุงููุงุฌูุฉ
const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, "ui"))); // ูุฌูุฏ ุงููุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ

// API Model
app.post("/run", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const r = await fetch(OLLAMA_API, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: MODEL,
        prompt: req.body.prompt,
        stream: false
      })
    });

    const data = await r.json();
    res.json({ reply: data.response });
  } catch {
    res.json({ reply: "โ๏ธ ูุดู ุงูุงุชุตุงู ุจุงูููุฏูู ุงููุญูู" });
  }
});

app.listen(PORT, () =>
  console.log(`๐ AGENT777-PRO ูุนูู โ Open โ  http://localhost:${PORT}`)
);
